> **The gated-aggregate mis-plan class + its indexes (HO 277ŌĆō279).** The same
> statless-planner trap hit a whole class of **summary-gated** fat-table
> COUNT/aggregates ŌĆö adding `AND summary IS NOT NULL` to a `bills` aggregate makes
> the planner drop it onto `idx_bills_is_ceremonial` (a `MULTI-INDEX OR` over
> ~every row, or a full scan), **slow even fully warm and wildly nondeterministic
> cold** (one query swung 112msŌåö18s+ across hits). It surfaced as live 10s-abort
> 500s on `/members` (HO 277), `/dashboard-v2` (HO 278, the swap blocker), and
> `/bills` (HO 279). The covering indexes (all `bills`, additive; in `migrate.ts`):
> - **`idx_bills_summary_feed (is_ceremonial, update_date) WHERE summary IS NOT NULL`** ŌĆö
>   the SHARED partial for the summary-gated `COUNT(*)`/`MAX(update_date)` shape:
>   `getFeedStats` (HO 277), `getCorpusStats(true)` (HO 278), and **`getFeedBills`'s
>   COUNT** (HO 279) all `INDEXED BY` onto it (their default WHERE all carry
>   `summary IS NOT NULL`). 12.1s ŌåÆ 38ms.
> - **`idx_bills_summary_stage (stage, is_ceremonial) WHERE summary IS NOT NULL`** ŌĆö
>   the gated stage distribution (HO 278); leading `stage` kills the temp-b-tree
>   GROUP BY. 860ms ŌåÆ 32ms. (The planner ALSO picks this one on its own for a
>   `?stage=` feed COUNT ŌĆö see the gating note below.)
> - **`idx_bills_summary_topics (is_ceremonial, topics) WHERE summary IS NOT NULL`** ŌĆö
>   the gated topic distribution (HO 278); `topics` in the index feeds `json_each`
>   index-only. 175ms ŌåÆ 38ms.
> - **`idx_bills_sponsor_agg (sponsor_bioguide_id, is_ceremonial, stage, congress)`** ŌĆö
>   the per-sponsor GROUP BY behind `/members` (HO 277): `billsAggCte`
>   (`getMembersRanked`). 3850ms ŌåÆ 96ms. (Was also `getSponsorProductivity`'s
>   index ŌĆö that helper was deleted in HO 328; the index stays for `billsAggCte`.)
> - **`idx_bills_sponsor_topics (sponsor_bioguide_id, is_ceremonial, topics) WHERE topics IS NOT NULL`** ŌĆö
>   the per-member topic-mix bar on the merged `/members` browser (HO 328): the
>   `json_each` fanout in `getMembersTopicMix`, grouped by `(sponsor_bioguide_id,
>   topic)`. Forced via `INDEXED BY`; makes the bills scan feeding `json_each`
>   index-only. ~5s cold (tipping the 10s abort) ŌåÆ fast. Safe only because the
>   query always constrains `sponsor_bioguide_id IS NOT NULL` + `topics IS NOT NULL`.
>
> **The hint is MANDATORY ŌĆö index alone is never enough** (the statless planner
> refused every one of these unhinted; confirmed 5├Ś). **And gate the hint NARROWLY
> to the exact path whose WHERE matches the partial's predicate.** A too-broad hint
> forces the WRONG index on a sibling path: HO 279's first cut hinted `getFeedBills`'s
> COUNT on every non-`cluster` path, which pessimized `/bills?stage=` (the planner's
> natural `idx_bills_summary_stage` SEARCH at 152ms ŌåÆ a forced `summary_feed`
> SCAN+row-fetch at 8.5s cold). Fixed by narrowing to the BARE gated case (no
> `stage`/`sponsor`/`q`/`chamber`/`topics`/`cluster`). **Verify the filtered/sibling
> paths after adding any hint**, not just the one you targeted.
>
> **`getFeedStats` is app-wide:** it's the masthead count rendered by `HeaderBar` on
> EVERY inner page, so its mis-plan was an app-wide 500 risk, not route-local ŌĆö
> fixing it (HO 277) protected every inner page at once.
>
> **HO 335 closed the rest of the class (the HO 332 site-wide EXPLAIN audit ŌĆö all
> 53 bills/news_mentions request-path statements).** Four more covering/partial
> `bills` indexes (in `migrate.ts`), each forced via `INDEXED BY`:
> - **`idx_bills_enacted (congress, latest_action_date) WHERE stage='enacted'`** ŌĆö
>   `getLawsEnactedBySessionWeek` (`/reports`) was a full SCAN of 16k for ~95 rows
>   (the audit's worst plan); now a covering congress lookup.
> - **`idx_bills_chamber_feed (bill_type, is_ceremonial) WHERE summary IS NOT NULL`** ŌĆö
>   `getFeedBills`'s `?chamber=` COUNT, index-only.
> - **`idx_bills_trends_month (congress, is_ceremonial, introduced_date, topics) WHERE topics IS NOT NULL`** ŌĆö
>   shared by `getBillsByMonth` + `getIntroductionsByMonth` (`/trends`), index-only.
> - **`idx_bills_chamber_topics (is_ceremonial, topics, bill_type)`** ŌĆö
>   `getTopicMixByChamber` (`/trends`); non-partial (the query is ungated); covering
>   incl. `bill_type` so the `json_each` driver is index-only.
>
> Plus hints onto EXISTING indexes (no new write cost): `getFeedBills`'s bare- and
> chamber-only row-SELECT ŌåÆ `idx_bills_latest_action` / `idx_bills_introduced_date`
> chosen by sort key (pre-ordered walk, LIMIT short-circuits ŌĆö closes the HO 279
> row-SELECT WATCH); `searchBills` ŌåÆ was hinted to `idx_bills_summary_feed` (HO
> 335) but the title/summary LIKE itself was the >10s wall ŌĆö **HO 336 replaced it
> with the `bills_fts` FTS5 index** (see the Full-text search box below); `getNewsFeed` (├Ś3) +
> `searchNews` ŌåÆ `news_mentions m INDEXED BY idx_news_mentions_published` (drive
> from the 227-row news side, not the 16k bills side ŌĆö the drive-order trap, see
> oddities). **Dead code deleted, not indexed** (the Group-D rule HO 331 set):
> `getBreakingNews`, `getSponsorsRanked`, `getSponsorPassRates`, `getSponsors`,
> `getSponsorCount`, and **`getStaleCount`** ŌĆö the last closes the HO 241 banked
> `/stale`-count loop by removal (no caller since HO 323/326; deleting beats
> indexing dead code). The 3 ungated `/dashboard-classic` dashboard reads are
> covering index-only MULTI-INDEX ORs (acceptable) and ride that route's sunset loop.
>
> **Discipline ŌĆö the merge-time check that ends the whack-a-mole:** any query that
> touches `bills` MUST EXPLAIN to an index-only plan (covering-index point lookup,
> index range, or covering-index scan) ŌĆö never an `idx_bills_is_ceremonial`
> MULTI-INDEX OR or a fat-table SCAN. A *covering* MULTI-INDEX OR (both
> `(is_ceremonial=0 OR IS NULL)` branches on a covering non-ceremonial index) is
> fine ŌĆö it's index-only. The standing probe is
> **`scripts/diagnostic/cold-start-audit-332.ts`** (EXPLAINs every bills/news_mentions
> request-path statement against prod, flags the failure signal, target 0 BAD); run
> it after adding or changing any `bills` query.
>
> **The bar is `USING COVERING INDEX`, not just `USING INDEX` (HO 340).** A plain
> `USING INDEX` that EXPLAIN renders as a clean `(col=?)` seek can still **row-fetch
> a huge fraction of the corpus** when the predicate is low-selectivity ŌĆö
> `getUnmatchedClusterCount`'s `cluster_id IS NULL` matched ~15k of 16.5k rows,
> rendered identically to a point lookup, and ran 20s while reading GOOD to two
> audits. EXPLAIN cannot show selectivity, so a non-COVERING index scan in an
> **unbounded aggregate** (COUNT/SUM/GROUP BY/DISTINCT, no LIMIT) is a *timing*
> question, not a plan one. The probe now emits **WARN** for that shape (run it with
> `TIME_WARN=1` to resolve each WARN by a warm timing ŌĆö >2s = the row-fetch trap).
> Fix = a covering index that carries the aggregated/filtered columns (HO 340:
> `idx_bills_cluster_agg (cluster_id, is_ceremonial, stage)` made both /patterns
> cluster queries index-only, 20s/4.7s ŌåÆ ~35ms). Same lesson as the /search LIKE,
> generalized: a clean plan ŌēĀ a fast query; an unbounded aggregate must be COVERING.
>
> **Full-text search goes through `bills_fts` (FTS5), NEVER a LIKE over title/summary
> (HO 336).** A leading-`%` `LIKE '%term%'` over the fat text columns full-scans all
> 16k rows and cold-aborts past the 10s limit regardless of any index (no index
> serves a leading wildcard). `bills_fts` is an external-content FTS5 index over
> `title/summary/sponsor_name` (NOT `id` ŌĆö its tokens 119/hr/number are in ~every id,
> so a prefix like `1*` expands to the whole index and blows up); `searchBills`/
> `searchBillsCount` build a prefix-token `MATCH` (`buildBillsFtsMatch`: alphanumeric
> tokens, `len>=3` ŌåÆ `tok*`, shorter ŌåÆ exact) and rank by `bm25`. Triggers
> (`bills_fts_ai/ad/au`) keep it synced across the sync upsert + the summarize UPDATE.
> Populate in **500-row rowid chunks**, never a one-shot `INSERT INTO bills_fts(bills_fts)
> VALUES('rebuild')` ŌĆö that reindexes 16k in one statement and the 10s `boundedFetch`
> aborts it mid-flight, leaving the external-content index `SQLITE_CORRUPT` (HO 336
> learned this twice). Recovery if it corrupts: drop the triggers + `bills_fts`,
> recreate, repopulate in chunks (what `migrate.ts` does on an empty index).
>
> **Both search surfaces use `bills_fts` (HO 338 extended it to the feed filter).**
> `/search` (the standalone `searchBills`/`searchBillsCount` helpers) AND `/bills?q=`
> (the inline feed filter inside `getFeedBills`) MATCH the index. **The feed filter
> has a q-present vs q-absent index split ŌĆö do NOT collapse it:** when `q` is set,
> `getFeedBills` drives from `bills_fts` (MATCH + `JOIN bills ON bills.rowid =
> bills_fts.rowid`), ANDs the other filters via `buildFeedWhere(filters, {prefix:
> "bills.", skipQ: true})`, and carries **no `INDEXED BY` hint** ŌĆö forcing the HO 335
> sort index there makes the planner drive the sort index instead of the FTS join,
> collapsing back to a scan. When `q` is absent, it's the HO 335 path verbatim
> (sort-conditional `idx_bills_latest_action` / `idx_bills_introduced_date` walk). The
> next person who "tidies" the feed by hinting the q path, or by routing both paths
> through one query, re-breaks `/bills?q=`. (The feed q-path date-sorts the matched
> set ŌĆö feed semantics ŌĆö vs `/search`'s bm25.)
>
> **Audit refinement (HO 336): the EXPLAIN probe is blind to full-corpus scans by
> construction.** `cold-start-audit-332.ts` prices the *plan*, and a leading-`%` LIKE
> or an unbounded aggregate has a plan that reads fine (a single index/table SCAN) ŌĆö
> the cost is the runtime wall-time of scanning every row, which EXPLAIN doesn't show.
> That's why the 332 audit passed `searchBills` while it 500'd. Plan-clean ŌēĀ fast:
> any query that touches the whole corpus by design needs a **runtime bounded-fetch
> timing check**, not just an EXPLAIN.

- `getFeedBills(filters, {page, pageSize})` ŌĆö main feed; returns `{ bills, total, page, pageSize, totalPages }`. `total` is the filtered count. The page passes `total` into `HeaderBar` via `feedFilteredCount` so the header doesn't need a second COUNT query. The unfiltered count for the "X of Y" header line comes from `getFeedStats().total`. SELECTs the HO 188 enrichment columns `sponsor_bioguide_id` + `cosponsor_count`, and (HO 192) `LEFT JOIN members msp ON msp.bioguide_id = bills.sponsor_bioguide_id` projecting `msp.depiction_url AS sponsor_depiction_url` for the sponsor hover card ŌĆö plus **HO 194's `msp.first_name`/`last_name`/`district` (as `sponsor_first_name`/`sponsor_last_name`/`sponsor_district`)** for the refined card's natural-order name + district, all on the *same* JOIN (no new query). Mirrors `getSponsorProductivity`'s join; `members.bioguide_id` is the PK so it's 1:1 (no row multiplication, and `total` is a separate JOIN-free COUNT anyway). All of these ride on `FeedBill` and are wired into `getFeedBills` only, so they degrade to absent on the other feed-shaped queries (`/stale`/`/changes`/`/watchlist`).
- `getStaleBills(filters, limit)` ŌĆö `/stale` page row list. Composes `buildStaleWhere` on top of the shared `buildFeedWhere`; the stale criteria (`latest_action_date IS NOT NULL`, `< date('now', '-60 days')`, `stage IN (introduced, committee, floor, other_chamber, other)`) are added to whatever the user filtered by. Sorted `latest_action_date ASC`, forced `INDEXED BY idx_bills_latest_action`. **`getStaleCount` was deleted in HO 335** (dead since HO 323/326 removed the count badge + its call) ŌĆö `/stale` shows no count.
- **President desk-time view** ŌĆö `/president` redirects to `/bills?stage=president` (HO 151). The dedicated `getPresidentBills` / `getPresidentCount` / `buildPresidentWhere` helpers were **deleted in HO 154.1** as orphans of that redirect; do not reference them. The desk-time column + oldest-at-desk ordering now ride `getFeedBills`: when the feed page detects `stage=president` as the sole active stage with no explicit `?sort`, it passes `direction: "asc"` (ŌåÆ `ORDER BY latest_action_date ASC NULLS LAST, id DESC`, oldest at desk first ŌĆö closest to the 10-day veto deadline) and `daysSinceMode="desk-time"` to `BillRowList`. `FeedFilters.direction` is internal-only ŌĆö never written by URL params, never surfaced in `SortDropdown`.
- `getStageChanges(filters, days=7, limit=200, dashboard?)` / `getStageChangesCount(filters, days)` ŌĆö `/changes` page and the dashboard's `ActivityTicker` (the **MOVERS** tab as of HO 232). `buildChangesWhere` composes on `buildFeedWhere` (stripping `filters.stage`) and adds `stage_changed_at` within the last `days`, sorted `stage_changed_at DESC`. Excludes ceremonial by default like everything built on `buildFeedWhere`, so the ticker calls it with empty `filters` + `limit: 15`. The optional 4th `DashboardFilters` arg carries the dashboard's click-to-filter state: `stage` matches transitions where `stage = ? OR previous_stage = ?` (either direction), `topic` narrows via `json_each` EXISTS. `/changes` ignores the 4th arg.
- `getEnactedThisWeek()` (HO 232) ŌĆö bills that reached `enacted` in the last 7 days. `unstable_cache` tag `bills`. The predicate lives in `lib/enacted-this-week.ts::queryEnactedThisWeek` (the single source) ŌĆö **two consumers, deliberately split:** the dashboard-lead cron reads it **raw** (it runs post-summarize, pre-`revalidateTag`, so a cached read would be stale), while the dashboard reads this **cached** helper. **HO 244 folded the standalone `EnactedBanner` into the new `WeeklyBand`** (`EnactedBanner.tsx` deleted) ŌĆö the enacted count + first Ōēż3 IDs now render as the band's `ŌŚÅ n ENACTED ┬Ę S n` segment (`--stage-enacted` green, linking `/bills?stage=enacted`); the N=0 state still renders visibly by design. `WeeklyBand` is the lone consumer now.
- `getDashboardPrimaries()` (HO 233) ŌĆö the PRIMARIES tab's 6-month rollup (`RacesPanelTabs` ŌåÆ `DashboardPrimaries`). **UNCACHED plain `db.execute`** ŌĆö the primaries surfaces are deliberately untagged (no revalidate tag exists, verified live), so this matches the `getUpcomingPrimaries` convention rather than inventing one. Returns `{ strip, cards, windowStart, windowEnd }` from one windowed `PRIMARY_SELECT` read: the strip is `primary_date ŌåÆ contest count` over `today..+6mo` (the soonest 4 dates flagged `soon`); the cards are those 4 dates with states + count + marquee seats. **"Rated" rides a derived seatId ŌåÆ `race_ratings` EXISTS, NOT `primaries.race_id`** (a dead link, 3/907 populated).
- `getSponsors` / `getSponsorCount` / `getSponsorsRanked` / `getSponsorPassRates` + the `SponsorFilters`/`Sponsor`/`SponsorRanking`/`SponsorPassRate` types and `buildSponsorWhere` ŌĆö **all deleted in HO 335** (dead code, orphaned by the HO 328 members/committees merge). The live `/members` roster is `getMembersRanked` (members Ō¤Ģ `billsAggCte`); the live per-sponsor surface is `getSponsorStats`/`getSponsorTopTopics`/`getSponsorRecentBills` (expand card) + `getSponsorStates` (dropdown).
- `getSponsorStates()` ŌĆö distinct non-null `sponsor_state` values (alphabetical) for the State dropdown.
- `getSponsorStats(key, includeCeremonial)` / `getSponsorTopTopics(key, limit, includeCeremonial)` / `getSponsorRecentBills(key, includeCeremonial)` ŌĆö the three per-sponsor aggregates behind the `/members` expand panel (5-query `Promise.all`). **`key` is a `bioguide_id` (HO 331).** Each filters `sponsor_bioguide_id = ?` and is **forced `INDEXED BY`** a covering index ŌĆö `idx_bills_sponsor_agg` (stats + recent-bills) / `idx_bills_sponsor_topics` (top-topics). **HO 331 retired the old `(sponsor_bioguide_id = ? OR sponsor_name = ?)` fallback:** the `sponsor_name` branch was unindexed and dead (the sole caller always passes a bioguide), and it dropped the statless planner onto `idx_bills_is_ceremonial` (MULTI-INDEX OR over ~every non-ceremonial row ŌåÆ cold-abort 500, the HO 277/329 misplan class). **Do NOT reintroduce an `OR sponsor_name` branch** ŌĆö it walks the fat table again. The hint is mandatory (the planner won't pick it unhinted); keep the `sponsor_bioguide_id` constraint or SQLite throws "no query solution". All three `unstable_cache` tag `bills`.
- `normalizePartyVariant(party)` ŌĆö collapses any sponsor party string to `'R' | 'D' | 'I' | null`. Use this both for filtering and for badge rendering so `R`, `D`, and everything-else-non-null map to the three party colors.
- `sanitizeStaleStage(input)` ŌĆö accepts only the four dropdown-eligible stages so a hand-typed `?stage=enacted` is silently ignored on `/stale`.
- `sanitizeSort(input)` ŌĆö accepts `'action' | 'introduced'`, falls back to `'action'` on anything else.
- `sanitizeIncludeCeremonial(input)` ŌĆö `'1'` ŌåÆ `true`, anything else ŌåÆ `false`. Default behavior hides ceremonial bills.
- `sanitizeClusterId(input)` ŌĆö returns the slug only if it matches a known `CLUSTER_PATTERNS` id (from `lib/cluster-patterns.ts`); anything else ŌåÆ `undefined`. URL input is untrusted everywhere.
- `getStageDistribution(filters?)` ŌĆö dashboard stage funnel: per-stage counts of substantive (non-ceremonial) on-path bills, plus `offPath` (stage `other`/NULL) and `total`. Optional `DashboardFilters` arg: `topic` re-shapes the funnel to that topic's stage distribution (via `json_each` EXISTS); `stage` is *not* applied here ŌĆö a single-bar funnel is useless, so `stage` only drives the component's selection state. Cached, tag `bills`, key includes the filter args.
- `getCorpusStats()` ŌĆö total non-ceremonial bill count + most recent `update_date`. **Feeds the HO 244 masthead stat readout** (`n bills tracked ┬Ę ŌĆ”`); its per-segment counts (in committee / on the floor / other chamber / enacted) come from `getStageDistribution`, which shares the same non-ceremonial predicate. Cached, tag `bills`, invalidated by the sync cron. **Count-predicate divergence (NOT a bug ŌĆö do not "fix"):** this readout total is non-ceremonial *including unsummarized* (~16,289), while inner pages' "BILLS" count additionally gates `summary IS NOT NULL` (~15k); the ~1k gap is unsummarized bills. The dashboardŌåöinner divergence is owned by the queued **masthead-coherence diagnostic**, not a defect.
- `getNewBillsThisWeekCount()` (HO 246) ŌĆö count of non-ceremonial bills with `introduced_date` in the last 7 days; powers the `WeeklyBand` NEW BILLS metric. **Forces `INDEXED BY idx_bills_introduced_date`** (the query always constrains `introduced_date`, so the hint is safe) ŌĆö 6838ms ŌåÆ 52ms cold; see the forced-index box above. Cached, tag `bills`.
- `getNewBillsThisWeek()` (HO 249) ŌĆö the LIST behind the **NEW THIS WEEK** tab (the third `ActivityTabs` tab, `NewThisWeek variant="v2"`, on `/dashboard-v2`'s RIGHT feed). Non-ceremonial bills introduced in the last 7 days, newest first, as `FeedBill` rows (same shape the MOVERS feed renders). Distinct from `getNewBillsThisWeekCount` (the WeeklyBand metric). Cached, tag `bills`.
- `getTopicDistribution(filters?)` ŌĆö corpus-wide topic counts (non-ceremonial only), sorted by count desc. Uses `json_each` to UNNEST the `topics` JSON array ŌĆö the standard pattern for aggregating across a JSON column; any future JSON columns aggregate the same way. Rows are validated against the `Topic` enum (unknown values logged and skipped). Optional `DashboardFilters` arg: `stage` narrows the counts to bills at that stage; `topic` is *not* applied here (visual selection only). Cached, tag `bills`, key includes the filter args.
- `getTopicMixByChamber()` ŌĆö chamber-faceted variant of the same topic distribution (handoff 76). Two `CASE WHEN bills.bill_type IN (...)` sums (house: `hr/hjres/hconres/hres`; senate: `s/sjres/sconres/sres`) over the same `json_each` fanout. Non-ceremonial, corpus-wide, tag `bills`. Every bill maps to exactly one chamber so the two sums never double-count. Sorted by combined count DESC so House and Senate columns share an axis. Backs `TopicMixByChamber` on the home dashboard.
- `getDashboardLead()` ŌĆö reads the current `weekly_lead` row from `dashboard_state` (`{ text, updatedAt }`), or `null` if the cron hasn't generated one yet. Cached, tag `bills`, invalidated by the cron after a fresh lead is written. **ORPHANED as of HO 244 ŌĆö deprecated-candidate, do NOT remove.** When the masthead became the stat readout (HO 244) nothing renders the lead anymore; the cron still generates it every tick. Retiring the generator vs. re-homing a glance one-liner is a pending design call ŌĆö leave both the helper and the generator in place until then.
- `getReportsWithLead(limit, offset)` / `getReportCount()` / `getReport(slug)` / `getDashboardReportSnapshot()` ŌĆö weekly reports for `/reports`, `/reports/[slug]`, and the dashboard `WeeklyBand`. **`getDashboardReportSnapshot()` SURVIVES the HO 244 redesign** ŌĆö the `ReportSnapshot` component it once backed was deleted, but the query now feeds the `WeeklyBand`'s READ FULL ŌåÆ target (returns `{ latest }`, `LIMIT 1`). All cached with tag `reports` (separate from `bills` because the cron's report step revalidates independently). The cron's Monday step calls `revalidateTag('reports')` after writing. `getReportsWithLead` is the paginated `/reports` list, each row carrying an `extractReportLead`-derived excerpt (HO 153). The pre-HO-153 lightweight `getReportsList()` / `getReports(limit, offset)` were **deleted in HO 154.1** ŌĆö do not reference them (this entry previously listed them as live; corrected in the HO 160 sweep).
- `getMember(bioguideId)` / `getMemberStats(bioguideId)` / `getMemberBills(bioguideId, limit)` ŌĆö back the `/members/[bioguideId]` member hub. Cached with tag `members` (24h revalidate); `getMemberBills` additionally tagged `bills` since the underlying bill rows change with the daily cron. `getMemberStats` excludes ceremonial bills from the enacted-rate denominator so the number reflects substantive work. `getSponsors` (`/members`) returns `sponsor_bioguide_id` via `MAX(...)` so the row's expanded panel can render `[View detail ŌåÆ]` when present.
- `getMemberAffiliations(bioguideId)` ŌĆö caucus affiliations for a member, sorted by `CAUCUS_CONFIG.priority` asc. Rows whose `org` is not in `CAUCUS_CONFIG` are filtered out (defensive against config renames leaving orphan rows). Cached tag `members`, shares the existing sync invalidation ŌĆö affiliations themselves are seeded manually, so no separate invalidation surface.
- `getRace(id)` / `getRaceCandidates(raceId)` ŌĆö back the `/race/[id]` hub **and the dashboard competitive-races 2├Ś2 hover popover** (HO 178 ŌĆö the hub data is server-prefetched in `CompetitiveRacesBlock` and passed as props, so `GET /api/race/[id]/hub` is no longer called by the dashboard; the endpoint is left in place, now unused by this surface). Both cached, tag `races`. `getRaceCandidates` orders by status precedence ŌĆö `won_primary` first, then `running`, `declared`, `withdrew`, others ŌĆö then name (`race_candidates` has no eliminated/lost status, so `withdrew` is the canonical "out" value). **HO 171** seeded `race_candidates` for the 4 strip races; **HO 174** refreshed them post-primary (PA-10 Stelson `won_primary`; GA Collins/Dooley `running` advanced, Carter `withdrew` eliminated; NJ-07 field corrected to Bennett/Roth/Shah/Varela, O'Rourke removed); **HO 182** then resolved NJ-07 post-primary ŌĆö Bennett `won_primary` (Dem nominee), Roth/Shah/Varela `withdrew`, general matchup Kean (R, incumbent) vs. Bennett (D). Challengers only ŌĆö the incumbent stays on the race row/card; Carter `C001103` + Collins `C001129` carry bioguides so they link to their member hubs. The `/api/revalidate?tag=races` route is the manual-flush hook; the seed scripts don't POST it ŌĆö hit it after a seed run.
- `getRaceRatings(raceId)` / `getMostCompetitiveRaces(cycle, limit)` ŌĆö back the rating chips on `/race/[id]` and the member-hub seat-up indicator (handoff 71). Both cached, tag `race-ratings` (separate from `races` because the rating seed refreshes quarterly on a different cadence). `getRaceRatings` returns rows sorted by `updated_at DESC`, so consumers can take `[0]` for the freshest read across sources. `getMostCompetitiveRaces` orders by `MIN(ABS(rating_score))` per race (so a single Toss Up rating from any source floats the race up), tiebreak `MAX(updated_at)`; **as of HO 163 it backs the dashboard competitive-races block** (`CompetitiveRacesBlock`, a Senate-led chamber mix ŌĆö a **2├Ś2 hover-popover card grid as of HO 178**; see the `/` entry). The `/api/revalidate?tag=race-ratings` route is the manual flush hook after a re-seed.
- `getRecentVotes(chamber, limit)` ŌĆö last N votes for one chamber, used by the (planned) dashboard ticker / chamber-level views. **Takes chamber, not bioguideId** ŌĆö sponsor-page vote lists use `getMemberVotes` instead. Cached, tag `votes`.
- `getVotesByBill(billId)` ŌĆö every vote tied to a specific bill (newest first). Backs the bill detail page's vote section. Cached, tag `votes`.
- `getMemberVote(voteId, bioguideId)` ŌĆö single position lookup; returns `{ position } | null`. Used inside the vote detail breakdown where one member's stance is highlighted. Cached, tag `votes`.
- `getMemberVotes(bioguideId, { page, pageSize })` ŌĆö paginated vote history for the member hub. **No chamber filter** ŌĆö joins `member_votes ŌåÆ votes` purely on bioguide_id, so House and Senate votes flow through the same list. Natural separation happens because a House member has no senate `member_votes` rows and vice versa. Cached, tag `votes`.
- `getMemberVoteStats(bioguideId)` ŌĆö yea/nay/present/not_voting totals for a member. Powers the `MemberVoteStats` line on the sponsor hub. Cached, tag `votes`.
- `getCommitteeActivityByPeriod(systemCode)` / `getCommitteeTopicMix(systemCode)` ŌĆö HO 146 chart helpers for `/committee/[systemCode]`. `getCommitteeActivityByPeriod` returns `{ month, bucket, count }[]` with `month = substr(activity_date, 1, 7)` and `bucket` one of `Referred | Markup | Reported | Other`, scoped to the current Congress via `congress = (SELECT MAX(congress) FROM bills)`. **Activity-type case-duplicate:** `committee_bills.activity_type` carries both `"Discharged From"` and `"Discharged from"` (case-different rows from the Congress.gov feed); the bucket-collapse expression uses `LOWER(activity_type)` so they normalize together ŌĆö any future raw-type matchers must use the lowercased form. `getCommitteeTopicMix` returns `{ topic, count }[]` via `json_each(bills.topics)` fanout with `COUNT(DISTINCT cb.bill_id)` (a referred-then-reported bill counts once), excludes ceremonial bills, no congress filter (matches `getTopicMixByChamber` corpus convention). Both `unstable_cache` tag `committees`.
- `getCommittees(filters?)` / `getCommitteeBills(systemCode, limit?, sinceDays?)` / `getCommitteeMembers(systemCode)` / `getCommitteeActivity(days?)` ŌĆö HO 143 data-layer helpers. All cached tag `committees`; `/api/cron/committees` calls `revalidateTag("committees")` to flush. `getCommitteeBills` returns `CommitteeBillRow[]` (`{ bill: FeedBill; activityType; activityDate }`) so a consumer can render per-committee activity context alongside the bill ŌĆö extended in HO 144 with an optional `sinceDays` argument that adds `AND activity_date >= datetime('now', '-<n> days')` to the inner CTE so `/committee/[systemCode]` can ask for "last 30 days" without filtering JS-side. The matching `activity_type` for the row's `MAX(activity_date)` is pulled via a correlated subquery so a bill referred and later reported still surfaces once with the freshest verb.
- `getMemberCommittees(bioguideId)` / `getBillCommittees(billId)` ŌĆö HO 145 cross-link helpers feeding the member-hub "Committees" section and the bill-detail "Committees" section. Both cached, tag `committees`. `getMemberCommittees` joins `committee_members` ŌåÆ `committees` ŌåÆ (parent committee for the `Ōå│ Parent` caption), filtered to `c.is_current = 1` and ordered parents-first by committee-type priority (Standing ŌåÆ Select ŌåÆ Joint ŌåÆ Task Force ŌåÆ Other) then by name, with subcommittees in a second block ordered by parent name then own name. `getBillCommittees` joins `committee_bills` ŌåÆ `committees` ŌåÆ parent and sorts by `activity_date DESC NULLS LAST, c.name ASC`. Rows are NOT deduped ŌĆö a `Referred to ŌåÆ Reported by` sequence on the same committee carries two informationally distinct rows. Rows with NULL `activity_date` or `activity_type` are dropped at read time so the return type can declare both as non-null strings (the schema allows NULLs).
- `getCommitteesIndex(filters?)` / `getCommitteeBySystemCode(systemCode)` / `getCommitteeSubcommittees(parentSystemCode)` ŌĆö HO 144 helpers for the `/committees` index and `/committee/[systemCode]` detail pages. `getCommitteesIndex` does the per-committee `member_count` + `recent_count` aggregates in a single SQL via two LEFT JOIN subqueries so the index renders 235 rows without N+1. Sort is computed in SQL (`activity` ŌåÆ `recent_count DESC, c.name ASC`; `name` ŌåÆ `c.name ASC`; `members` ŌåÆ `member_count DESC, c.name ASC`); chamber filter is one optional `AND c.chamber = ?`. `is_current = 1` is hardcoded ŌĆö there is no toggle for retired committees on the index. `getCommitteeBySystemCode` is a single-row lookup (returns `Committee | null`); `getCommitteeSubcommittees` lists current rows where `parent_system_code = ?`. All cached, tag `committees`. Companion sanitizers: `sanitizeCommitteeChamber` (validates against `house|senate|joint`), `sanitizeCommitteeSort` (validates against `activity|name|members`, falls back to `activity`).
- `getUpcomingMeetings(opts?)` / `getRecentMeetings(days?)` / `getMeetingsByCommittee(systemCode, opts?)` / `getMeetingsForBill(billId)` ŌĆö **HO 263 committee-meetings (hearings) read layer, Phase 1 ŌĆö NO UI yet** (a `/hearings` calendar + committee-detail "this week" + bill-hub "hearings covering this bill" go to Design then a later build handoff). All return `CommitteeMeeting[]` (`{eventId, chamber, meetingDate, meetingType, meetingStatus, title, building, room, videoUrl, committeeSystemCode, bills: FeedBill[]}`). `getUpcomingMeetings` = `meeting_date >= now` ASC (the calendar spine; the source only runs ~2 weeks ahead, HO 261); `getRecentMeetings` = last `days` DESC; `getMeetingsByCommittee` filters one committee (`upcomingOnly` ŌåÆ future ASC, else all DESC); `getMeetingsForBill` is the reverse lookup. The `bills` array comes from `meeting_bills ŌåÆ bills` joined in SQL + grouped in JS (ONE extra query per helper, not an N+1) ŌĆö sparse by nature (~20% House / ~12% Senate carry a bill), and a meeting referencing a not-yet-synced bill drops out of the INNER JOIN (honest degrade, no chip). All cached, **tag `meetings`** (the 12th tag; `/api/cron/committees` revalidates it after the meetings step). **Sync** (`lib/meetings-sync.ts::syncMeetings`, mirrors `committees-sync.ts`): the list endpoint is updateDate-DESC with no date filter and the meeting DATE lives only on the detail record, so the cursor is a per-chamber `meeting_sync_state` watermark ŌĆö collect the thin list newestŌåÆoldest until the synced tail, process oldest-first (detail fetch per event), advance the watermark per completed event (committing every 50 for crash-safety, HO 120 pattern). **video_url** = the `videos[]` entry whose host is NOT `api.congress.gov` (YouTube for House, senate.gov/isvp for Senate), null when absent. **Bill join = `relatedItems.bills[]` only** (clean `{congress,type,number}`); the messier `meetingDocuments` PDF-name parse is deliberately NOT used in v1. **No `raw_json`** on either table (the HO 241 bloat lesson). The `CONGRESS_API_KEY` is `.trim()`'d (the local `.env` has a trailing space that breaks the URL). **HO 273 ŌĆö meeting titles are cleaned at RENDER via `cleanMeetingTitle()` in `lib/hearings.ts`:** deterministic string rules (no LLM) strip Senate procedural lead-ins ("Hearings to examineŌĆ”", "Business meeting to considerŌĆ”", "To receive a closed briefing onŌĆ”", markups, oversight/legislative hearings), drop a leftover leading "the", re-capitalize, and fall back to the raw title if a strip empties it. Raw titles stay in the DB; the meeting TYPE is already carried by the badge, so dropping the lead-in loses nothing. All three render sites import the ONE helper ŌĆö `HearingRow`, `HearingsCalendar`, `OnTheHillBand` ŌĆö don't re-clean at ingest and don't duplicate the regex. NBSP/narrow-NBSP (U+00A0/U+202F) are normalized to a plain space FIRST, else a literal-space prefix silently fails to match (see oddities.md).

### Ceremonial filter (`?ceremonial=1`)

`FeedFilters.includeCeremonial?: boolean` and `SponsorFilters.includeCeremonial?: boolean` flow through `buildFeedWhere` / `buildSponsorWhere`. Both helpers append `(is_ceremonial = 0 OR is_ceremonial IS NULL)` unless the flag is true. NULL counts as visible during backfill so the dashboard doesn't go dark while the classifier is running. The flag becomes part of the `unstable_cache` argument-derived key, so the on/off variants live in separate cache slots.

Don't apply on `/watchlist` or `/bill/[id]` ŌĆö watched ceremonial bills must surface, and detail pages always render. The toggle is a list-view concept. `getFeedStats(includeCeremonial, cluster?)`, `getSponsorRecentBills(key, includeCeremonial)`, `getSponsorStats(key, includeCeremonial)`, and `getSponsorTopTopics(key, limit, includeCeremonial)` all take the flag explicitly so the expanded sponsor panel matches the active toggle.

### Cluster filter (`?cluster=<slug>`)

Regex-based template clustering. Patterns + `classifyCluster(title, billType)` live in `lib/cluster-patterns.ts` (single source of truth ŌĆö pattern revision is cheap because there's no separate metadata store). The sync upsert calls `classifyCluster` unconditionally on every bill (pure regex, zero cost) and writes `cluster_id` in the same `INSERT ... ON CONFLICT` statement.

`FeedFilters.cluster?: string` propagates through `buildFeedWhere`, which adds `cluster_id = ?`. **Cluster bypasses the ceremonial gate** ŌĆö when `cluster` is set, `buildFeedWhere` skips the `(is_ceremonial = 0 OR is_ceremonial IS NULL)` clause entirely. Reasoning: most clusters are mostly ceremonial; opting into "awareness designations" means asking to see the noise. The toggle is suppressed in `HeaderBar` whenever `feedFilters.cluster` is set so the dead control isn't rendered.

Sponsor queries do not take the cluster filter (sponsor page is about people, not bill shapes). `getClusterStats()` returns `[{id, name, description, count, exampleTitle}]` sorted by count desc; `getUnmatchedClusterCount(includeCeremonial)` returns `COUNT(*) WHERE cluster_id IS NULL` honoring the active ceremonial filter. Both cached `tags: ["bills"]`.

Backfill: `npm run backfill-clusters` ŌåÆ `scripts/backfill-clusters.ts`. Pure regex, no API calls; runs in under a minute against the full corpus. Idempotent via `WHERE cluster_id IS NULL` so re-running after adding a sixth pattern only touches previously-unmatched rows. Logs per-cluster counts at the end. POSTs to `REVALIDATE_URL` (with `Authorization: Bearer ${CRON_SECRET}`) on completion to invalidate the `bills` tag, same as the ceremonial backfill.

### Feed sort (`?sort=action|introduced`)

Applies to `/` and `/watchlist` only. Two keys, default `action`:

- `action`: `ORDER BY latest_action_date DESC NULLS LAST, id DESC`
- `introduced`: `ORDER BY introduced_date DESC NULLS LAST, id DESC`

`SortDropdown` is a client component that mirrors `StageFilter`. It deletes `expanded` and (for the default) `sort` from the URL on change, preserves everything else. The visible Action column always shows `latest_action_date` regardless of sort key ŌĆö the sort axis isn't what's displayed.

Do **not** add the dropdown to `/stale` (forced ASC by definition) or `/members` (sorted by `bill_count`, different axis). The `/bills?stage=president` alias keeps the dropdown ŌĆö picking an explicit `?sort` there is exactly what disables the desk-time/ASC alias path.

`FeedFilters` includes an optional `sponsor?: string`. When set, `buildFeedWhere` ANDs `sponsor_name = ?` so `/?sponsor=<encoded name>` filters the main feed. The HeaderBar count line shows `┬Ę sponsored by <name>` in `--accent-amber` when active. All other feed filters (stage, topics, q) compose with it via the same plumbing ŌĆö and the `StageFilter`, `TopicFilter`, `BillRow` components all thread `sponsor` through their generated hrefs, same way they thread `q`.

## Summarization prompt

Keep summaries 2-3 sentences. Plain English. Neutral. Focus on what the bill *does*, not what it's titled. The CRS summary is a useful input but should not be copied.

Prompt template:

```
You are summarizing a US Congress bill for a personal tracking dashboard. Write a 2-3 sentence summary in plain English that explains what the bill would actually change if enacted. Avoid legalese, avoid the bill's marketing title, avoid editorial language. State who is affected and how.

Then output a JSON block with:
- topics: array of 1-3 topic tags from this list: [healthcare, immigration, taxes, defense, energy, environment, education, labor, technology, civil_rights, criminal_justice, agriculture, trade, housing, transportation, foreign_policy, veterans, elections, budget, financial_services, government_operations, consumer_protection, social_security, other]
- stage: one of [introduced, committee, floor, other_chamber, president, enacted]
- is_ceremonial: true if symbolic (awareness days, building renamings, recognitions, sense-of-Congress); false if it changes law, appropriates funds, or directs an agency

Bill title: {title}
Latest action: {latest_action_text}
CRS summary (if any): {crs_summary}
Bill text (truncated): {bill_text_first_8000_chars}

Respond in this exact format:

SUMMARY:
<2-3 sentences>

JSON:
{"topics": [...], "stage": "...", "is_ceremonial": true|false}
```

Parse the response by splitting on `JSON:` and parsing the second half. If parsing fails, log the bill ID and skip it; don't crash the sync. The `is_ceremonial` field is defensive: if the model omits it or returns a non-boolean, the parser writes NULL so the standalone backfill (`npm run classify-ceremonial`) can pick it up later. Title-only re-classification lives in `lib/classify-ceremonial.ts`; the sync `UPSERT_SQL` clears `is_ceremonial` along with `summary` whenever `update_date` changes so re-classification rides through the inline summarize path with no extra Gemini call.

The prompt will need iteration. Expect to revise it 5-10 times. Common failure modes: LLM repeats the bill's marketing title, LLM editorializes, LLM picks `other` for the topic when a better tag exists. Test against a sample of 20 known bills and read the outputs side by side.

### Stage-monotonicity guard (HO 239)

The LLM classifies `stage` from `latest_action_text`, but the text can be ambiguous and the model can regress a bill. Two guards keep `stage` monotonic ŌĆö it only advances:

- **Prompt-side** (`lib/summarize.ts`, in the stage-rules block): (a) a bill never regresses to `introduced` once it has advanced past it ŌĆö when torn between `introduced` and a later stage for a bill already in motion, choose the later; (b) post-passage procedural actions (e.g. "motion to reconsider laid on the table", "motion to table agreed to") mean the chamber has already acted ŌĆö classify `floor` or later, never `introduced`/`committee`. (The live prompt also carries explicit *ordered* action-textŌåÆstage rules ŌĆö "Became Public Law"ŌåÆenacted, "Presented to President"ŌåÆpresident, both-chambers-passedŌåÆother_chamber, one-passedŌåÆfloor, "Reported"/"Referred to"ŌåÆcommittee, else introduced ŌĆö fuller than the simplified `JSON` template shown above; the template is stale on this and flagged for a future prompt-section refresh.)
- **Code-side** (`lib/summarize-runner.ts::decideStage(current, proposed, pending)` ŌåÆ `"advance" | "reject" | "pend" | "noop"`): ranks via `stageRank` (`lib/enums.ts` ŌĆö `ALLOWED_STAGES.indexOf`, introduced=0 ŌĆ” enacted=5, unlisted/null=ŌłÆ1). `proposed` ahead of `current` ŌåÆ **advance**, the ONLY path that writes `stage`/`previous_stage`/`stage_changed_at` and appends a `stage_transitions` row. A downgrade **to `introduced`** ŌåÆ **reject** (impossible regression; keeps the old stage, clears any pending, logs `[stage] rejected impossible downgrade`). Any **other** downgrade ŌåÆ **pend**: parked in `pending_stage`/`pending_stage_at`, and the slot does NOT move until a SECOND matching proposal confirms it (`proposed === pending` ŌåÆ advance) ŌĆö a two-tick vote so one noisy classification can't drag a bill backward. `noop` when unchanged or first-seen-`introduced`. On anything but `advance`, nothing touches `stage`/`previous_stage`/`stage_changed_at`/`stage_transitions`.

## Dashboard lead generation

The dashboard's top-of-page `DashboardLead` is a 3-sentence prose summary, generated once per cron tick by `lib/dashboard-lead.ts::generateDashboardLead`.

> **ORPHANED RENDER as of HO 244.** The masthead became a stat readout (`n bills tracked ┬Ę ŌĆ”`), so nothing renders this lead anymore ŌĆö but the cron **still generates and stores it every tick** (`getDashboardLead` is the deprecated-candidate read; see Query helpers). The generator below is intact; retiring it vs. re-homing the one-liner is a pending design call. Don't delete the pipeline.

- **Inputs:** corpus size, last-7-day stage transitions (count + top 5 with bill ID, truncated title, transition arrow), last-7-day enactments (count + top 3 IDs), last-7-day new introductions (count), and the topic with the most transitions in the last 7 days. All gathered by focused queries in `lib/dashboard-lead.ts` ŌĆö not cached UI helpers.
- **Model:** `gemini-2.5-flash`, single completion, reuses the `SUMMARY_MODEL` constant and client pattern from `lib/summarize.ts`.
- **Prompt** lives in source under `lib/dashboard-lead.ts`. Expect prompt iteration over the first 5-10 generations ŌĆö same failure modes as the summarize prompt (marketing-title creep, generic openers like "This week, Congress...", vague numbers, editorial framing).
- **Storage:** upserted into `dashboard_state` under `key = 'weekly_lead'` with a JS-side ISO `updated_at`. Read back by `getDashboardLead()`.
- **Cron integration:** `app/api/sync/route.ts` calls `generateDashboardLead` + `writeDashboardLead` after sync + summarize, then `revalidateTag("bills")`. Failure is non-fatal ŌĆö the cron logs a warning, the prior lead stays in the DB, and the dashboard keeps rendering it.
- **Manual run:** `npm run lead` ŌåÆ `scripts/generate-lead.ts` generates, prints, and writes a lead. Use it to iterate on the prompt without waiting for cron.

## Report generation

Weekly reports ŌĆö one Markdown blob per calendar week, rendered at `/reports/[slug]`.

- Generated weekly on Monday 09:30 UTC by `app/api/cron/weekly-report/route.ts`, which calls `lib/report-generation.ts::generateWeeklyReport`. HO 139 split this out of `/api/sync` after the shared Monday 09:00 tick repeatedly never reached the report step inside its 60s budget; the route now has the full ceiling to itself and the cron is Monday-only via the `30 9 * * 1` schedule.
- **Incomplete-week guard (HO 110):** `generateWeeklyReport` throws if `week.end` is in the future, so a report is never generated for a week that hasn't closed (the cron treats the throw as non-fatal and retries next tick). The 2026-05-18 backfilled row predates the guard and is left as a historical artifact.
- One Gemini call per report. Structured output with four section markers (`LEAD`, `STAGE_COMMENTARY`, `ENACTMENTS_COMMENTARY`, `MOST_TALKED_COMMENTARY`). Parsed by splitting on markers, same pattern as the summarize prompt. The `ENACTMENTS_COMMENTARY` and `STAGE_COMMENTARY` slots also carry the LLM's zero-count placeholder, though assembly owns the copy when a count is zero and ignores the LLM output there.
- The Markdown body is assembled programmatically: section headers + counts come from the data, prose comes from the LLM. Bill IDs render as plain text (`HR 2702`); stage transitions use the canonical `Ō¢Ė INTRO ŌåÆ Ō¢ĖŌ¢Ė COMMITTEE` glyphs.
- Storage: upserted into `reports` keyed by `slug` (the ISO week-start date). Re-running for the same week overwrites the prior row.
- Failure mode: cron logs a warning and writes no row; the sync's other steps still complete. Manual recovery: `npm run report` (prior week) or `npm run report YYYY-MM-DD` (specific week start). `scripts/generate-report.ts` prints the assembled Markdown before writing ŌĆö useful for iterating on the prompt.
- Notable introductions ranks by `cosponsor_count DESC NULLS LAST`, tiebroken by `COALESCE(text_length, 0) DESC` then `id DESC`. The pre-filter `(text_length IS NULL OR text_length > 5000)` excludes short resolutions and one-pagers that slip past the ceremonial+cluster gates while keeping NULL rows visible during backfill. CRA-disapproval is included as substantive; other clusters are filtered out. (The handoff-58 `LENGTH(summary)` proxy was retired in handoff 59.)
- Markdown rendered on `/reports/[slug]` via `react-markdown` + `remark-gfm` (needed for the topic-breakdown table) with terminal-aesthetic component overrides in `components/ReportMarkdown.tsx`.
- Bill IDs in a rendered report auto-link to `/bill/[id]` (HO 113): `ReportMarkdown` pre-substitutes bare IDs (`HR 2702`, `HJRES 140`, ŌĆ”) into markdown links before rendering, normalizing to the `{getCurrentCongress()}-{type}-{number}` `bills.id` form. A `[`-lookbehind prevents double-wrapping an already-linked ID; `(?!\d)` leaves a trailing `'s`/`s` outside the link.
- "Most talked about" is confidence-gated (HO 111): the `mostTalkedAbout` query keeps only `news_mentions` rows with `match_confidence >= 0.7` (which also excludes NULL-confidence rows ŌĆö SQL three-valued logic), and only bills with `>= 2` such mentions. Ranked by mention count ŌåÆ avg confidence ŌåÆ recency. The prompt context gets a bucketed `confidence_tier` (`high` >= 0.9, else `medium`) plus outlets and sample headlines ŌĆö never the raw float.
- The prose prompt (`SYSTEM_PROMPT` in `lib/report-generation.ts`, tuned HO 112) enforces a synthesis-not-recite LEAD, an anti-restate rule (prose states a section's significance, not the list's contents), confidence-tier verb guidance, no LLM-invented counts, and a banned-phrase list. `buildUserPrompt` feeds week-over-week introduction deltas and per-transition direction (forward/backward) as synthesis raw material. Gemini 2.5 Flash obeys imperfectly ŌĆö banned-word inflections still leak occasionally; further LEAD tuning is HO 112.1 territory.

### Report section anatomy (HO 352 / 358 / 360)

The body assembly (`buildReportMarkdown` in `lib/report-generation.ts`) carries two structured sections worth knowing the shape of, **in this order**:

- **Stage movements** (`## Stage movements (N)`) renders as a **destination-stage ladder** (HO 352) ŌĆö one rung per stage in canonical order (`LADDER_STAGES`; **`introduced` is NOT a rung** ŌĆö a fresh intro has no "advance into" story), sqrt-scaled bars reusing the dashboard stage-distribution bar, zero-count rungs kept dimmed. The **committee** rung is routine referrals, **count-only**; rungs past committee (floor+) name their bills on sub-lines, capped with a `+N more` tail (`rung.billTotal ŌłÆ rung.bills.length`). This replaced the old per-transition row list.
- **Floor votes** (`## Floor votes (N)`) sits **after** Stage movements (the natural read: what moved, then how the floor voted). Named decisive votes are one line each (`formatVoteLine`): **bold outcome verb** `PASSED / FAILED / ADVANCED / BLOCKED / CONFIRMED / REJECTED` ┬Ę chamber `S`/`H` ┬Ę bill ref (a **bare ID** like `HR 2702`, linkified to `/bill/119-ŌĆ”` by `ReportMarkdown`'s `linkifyBillIds`, **NOT** `/bills/slug`) or `nominee ŌåÆ position` ┬Ę margin `yeaŌĆōnay` (cloture-prefixed for ADVANCED/BLOCKED) ┬Ę party split (`D yŌĆōn ┬Ę R yŌĆōn`, with `I` only when notable) shown **only on contested/divergent** votes (`shouldShowSplit` ŌĆö diverging parties or a tight margin). The verb classifier (`classifyVote`) reads live `result` / `question` / `amendment_designation` ŌĆö no invented strings. Procedural / amendment / UC-nomination votes collapse to a `+ N more recorded vote(s)` line. Recess states are handled (`formatRecessLine`: one-chamber-dark line; both-in-session-no-votes; both-in-recess).
- **`content_md` is one pure-markdown string.** The web render (`ReportMarkdown`) and the `.md` download are identical **except one deliberate web-only divergence**: `ReportMarkdown` colors the outcome verb by **exact-text match** on the bolded token (`PASSED`/`CONFIRMED` ŌåÆ `--stage-enacted`; `ADVANCED` ŌåÆ `--stage-floor`; `FAILED`/`BLOCKED`/`REJECTED` ŌåÆ `--party-republican`); every other `<strong>` stays `--text-secondary`, so a bolded prose word never false-matches. The stored markdown carries **no color/HTML** ŌĆö just `**FAILED**` ŌĆö so the download is plain bold. (See oddities for why color can't live in `content_md`, and that the same rule could later re-color the 352 ladder's stage labels.)

## Frontend design system

Bloomberg Terminal aesthetic. Dark monospace, dense rows, color-coded stages and topics. No light mode. **Typeface rule ŌĆö mono for chrome, sans for prose (HO 299/300):** the app is monospace by default, but the **`--sans` token** (`system-ui, -apple-system, "Segoe UI", Roboto, sans-serif`) is now used for **PROSE in the v2 feed** ŌĆö bill titles, summaries, news headlines, sponsor names. **Mono stays for ALL chrome** ŌĆö chips, metrics, labels, IDs, dates, anything coded. This is the **first sans in CBT** (older comments in `globals.css` still say "no `--sans` in CBT" ŌĆö stale, predate the token); the convention now reads "mono for chrome, sans for prose," not mono-only. Tailwind v4 only (no shadcn / no other libraries). Server components by default. Client islands are now numerous (~53 `"use client"` components ŌĆö 55 `^"use client"` grep matches under `components/` incl. the 2 hook files `useSingleOpenPanel.ts` / `use-watch-toggle.ts`; **HO 328 added `CommitteeRailRow` + `RosterShowAll` (the `/members` rail rows + roster disclosure) and deleted `MemberProductivityScatter`** with the scatter; earlier: `CartogramShell` / `RaceMapCard` / `PrimaryMapCard` added HO 210) ŌĆö filter/URL chips (`StageFilter`, `PartyFilter`, `StateFilter`, `CeremonialToggle`, `SortDropdown`, `SearchBox`, `SearchTabs`), the feed + dashboard accordions (`BillRowList` / `BillRow` / `BillExpandedPanel` / `TopStallsList`), interactive charts (`DashboardTopicTreemap`, `StageFunnel`; the `/patterns` `PatternBars` ranked-bar list that replaced `PatternBubbleSVG` in HO 347 is a **server** component ŌĆö URL-driven `<Link>` rows, not an island), chrome (`MarketsTapeClient`, `CyclingTimestamp`, `ActivityTabs`, `Tooltip`, `MobileNavDrawer` ŌĆö dormant), and row affordances (`WatchlistToggle`, `WatchStar`, `MediaAttentionCell`, `MemberHeader`, `RaceIncumbentCard`, `StateFlag`, `SponsorPhoto`, `SponsorHoverName`). See `### Server / client split` for the canonical set.

Per-mode params don't collide; the other mode's params persist in the URL across switches (no aggressive clear). `BILLS` (`?mode=bills`): **25/page** (`FEED_PAGE_SIZE`, HO 187 ŌĆö down from 100, not the 50 this entry long claimed), `BillRowList` accordions (HO 148). **HO 187/189 restructured inner pages into 4 chrome bands** (see the HeaderBar / inner-chrome note): (1) the title bar (path + inline filter-aware sync + nav), (2) the **control strip** ŌĆö BILLS|NEWS toggle + `StageFilter` (ALL STAGES, includes `president`) + chamber `SegmentedToggle` (ALL/HOUSE/SENATE) + a **compact ŌīĢ `SearchBox`** (`flex:1`, max 230px) + **INCLUDE CEREMONIAL** + `SortDropdown` pinned right (search + ceremonial moved here out of the old HeaderBar masthead), (3) the **topics band** ŌĆö the feed sub-nav Changes┬ĘPresident┬ĘReports + a divider rule + the multi-select `TopicFilter` chips (comma-list `?topics=ŌĆ”`), (4) the **legend + pagination** band (`StageLegend` + `Pagination`). BILLS-only params: `stage`, `sponsor`, `chamber`, `ceremonial`, `cluster`, `q`, `topics`, `sort`. The only structurally shared param is `page`; `topics`/`sort` are BILLS-only but preserved in the URL across a mode switch (round-trip symmetry), not consumed by NEWS rendering. (Corrected in the HO 160 sweep ŌĆö the prior "shared `topics`/`sort`/`page`" framing conflated URL-preservation with cross-mode use.) `NEWS` (`?mode=news`): 50/page, `NewsRow` list inside the same `news-header-row` chrome the standalone `/news` used, `NewsFilters` chips for `SOURCE` (politico/the_hill/roll_call) + `WINDOW` (24/72/168/720h, default 72h) + single-select `TOPIC` (`?topic=ŌĆ”` singular, distinct from BILLS' plural) + a clearable `?bill=<id>` pill that scopes to one bill (drops window + confidence gate while scoped ŌĆö same as HO 130's per-bill semantics). NEWS-only params: `source`, `topic`, `window`, `bill`. SORT is a static "most recent" label ŌĆö no dropdown shell. `HeaderBar` runs in `pageTitle="News mentions"` + `pageCount=mentions` mode for NEWS, dropping the search box. Backed by `getNewsFeed({source?, topic?, windowHours?, billId?, page?, pageSize?})` which reuses `getBreakingNewsForHome`'s dedup-by-article-key + confidence floor (0.7) when not bill-scoped, paginates via OFFSET, tag `news-breaking`. Companion sanitizers: `sanitizeNewsSource`, `sanitizeWindowHours`. **President desk-time alias:** `/president` is now its **own in-surface page** (HO 359 ŌĆö see its entry; it no longer redirects here), but the `/bills?stage=president` alias path described here still applies for direct visits/power filtering ŌĆö when `stage=president` is the sole active stage AND no explicit `?sort` override, the feed page re-applies the legacy `daysSinceMode="desk-time"` desk-time column AND switches the SQL `ORDER BY` to ASC (oldest-at-desk first) ŌĆö the column and the order ship together so the visible signal stays coherent. `FeedFilters.direction?: "asc"` carries this through `getFeedBills`; it's internal-only, never written by URL params and never surfaced in `SortDropdown`. `getPresidentBills` / `getPresidentCount` were deleted in HO 154.1 as orphans of this redirect. **News alias absorbed:** `/news` redirects to `/bills?mode=news` (and `/news?bill=<id>` to `/bills?mode=news&bill=<id>`); `MediaAttentionCell` points directly at the new target. (The `/news` + `/president` alias `redirect()`s were retargeted straight to `/bills` in HO 184 to avoid a `/news ŌåÆ /feed ŌåÆ /bills` double-hop.) **Double-nav resolved (HO 184):** the BILLS|NEWS `SegmentedToggle` is the canonical mode switch; the `feed` GROUP_TABS row previously *also* carried Bills + News tabs (a redundant second way to switch the same mode), so they were dropped ŌĆö the feed sub-nav now reads **Changes ┬Ę President ┬Ę Reports** (sibling/derived views; Reports kept as a deliberate pre-existing special-case). Accepted tradeoff: in bills/news mode no sub-nav tab is active.
- `/bill/[id]` ŌĆö detail page (card panel layout). HO 145 added a **Committees** block between the field grid (Sponsor/Introduced/Last action/Stage/Topics) and the Summary, fed by `getBillCommittees(billId)`. Section is **skipped entirely** when the bill has no committee_bills rows (a normal state for fresh introductions / many resolutions ŌĆö a "no referrals" line would be noise). Each row links to `/committee/[systemCode]`, carries the chamber label, an `Ōå│ ParentName` caption for subcommittees, and an `Activity ┬Ę Xmo ago` suffix via `formatRelativeAgeLong`. No dedupe ŌĆö a referred-then-reported sequence shows two rows.
- `/watchlist` ŌĆö bills flagged via `Ōśģ Watch`
- `/stale` ŌĆö **stage-led "past committee" stalls (HO 350, supersedes the old oldest-first-all-stages view).** Default scope is the **past-committee group `stage IN ('floor','other_chamber','president')`** (`STALE_PAST_COMMITTEE_STAGES`, enacted excluded ŌĆö success isn't a stall), still gated to **60+ days** since last action (`STALE_DAYS=60`), sorted **legislative-stage DESC then furthest-action-first** (`latest_action_date ASC`). So the surface answers "what advanced past committee and then went quiet, ordered by how far it got," not "every old bill oldest-first." The header reads `past committee ┬Ę stalled 60+ days ┬Ę furthest first`. **Stage filter** (`STALE_FILTER_STAGES` = `introduced`/`committee`/`floor`/`other_chamber`; `president`/`enacted` not offered) lets you isolate a single stage ŌĆö picking one drops the default past-committee scope and shows just that stage (the index/sort flips accordingly; see the `getStaleBills` helper). A **committee-backlog footer** (`getStaleCommitteeCount`) renders `{N} more sit in committee ŌåÆ` linking to `?stage=committee` ŌĆö the committee wall is one click away, not the default. **Procedural-housekeeping filter (HO 350, `lib/stale-procedural.ts`):** the default view hides one-time opening-week organizational resolutions (they did their job ŌĆö not stalls). It's a curated hybrid: a **FROZEN id list** `STALE_PROCEDURAL_IDS` (13 items ŌĆö electoral-vote count, elect/notify officers, fix meeting hour, quorum/assemble, pro-tem election, **including the 3 joint-session resolutions** `hconres-11/16/74`) + a **LIVE title pattern** `STALE_PROCEDURAL_TITLE_PATTERN = "electing members%"` (anchored, for the recurring "Electing Members to ŌĆ” committees" family) + a **blocklist** `STALE_PROCEDURAL_BLOCKLIST` (`119-hres-966`, `119-sres-6` ŌĆö honoring/thanks resolutions that mention "President pro tempore" and must survive the pattern). The boundary: `hres-5` (the Rules package) and "Amending the Rules" resolutions are **never** filtered ŌĆö they're real, and the anchored `electing members%` pattern can't catch them. An **INCLUDE PROCEDURAL** toggle (`ProceduralToggle`, `?procedural=1`) is the escape hatch that reveals them in one click ŌĆö also the safety valve if the curation ever grabs a real bill. To extend, edit the three lists in `lib/stale-procedural.ts` (validated by `scripts/diagnostic/stale-procedural-350.ts`; signed off before the default shipped). Same filter chrome as the feed (topics/chamber/search/ceremonial). Action column renders days-since (`247d`) instead of a date, color-coded by threshold (`daysSinceMode="staleness"`).
- `/president` ŌĆö **HO 359: a real in-surface page** (the president's-desk sub-tab), no longer the HO 151 redirect to `/bills?stage=president`. Clicking PRESIDENT in the feed sub-nav used to dump the user onto the full `/bills` feed (sub-nav unmarked, breadcrumb under Bills); now `app/president/page.tsx` carries the **same chrome as `/changes`** (its sibling) ŌĆö `HeaderBar` + the feed `GroupTabs` sub-nav (Changes ┬Ę President ┬Ę Reports, with the **active tab marked**) + `StageLegend` + `BillRowList` ŌĆö so the tab keeps you in-surface. Data is unchanged: president-stage bills, oldest-at-desk-first (`direction:"asc"`, racing the 10-day veto clock) with the `daysSinceMode="desk-time"` days-since column ŌĆö the exact semantics the `/bills?stage=president` alias still applies for direct visits / power filtering. Breadcrumb `Bills\President` (`lib/breadcrumb.ts`).
- `/changes` ŌĆö bills whose stage moved in the last 7 days, sorted by `stage_changed_at DESC` (the `getStageChanges` predicate). The "in motion" view between `/stale` and `/president`. No stage filter (the page is about transitions, not destinations). Topic + search + chamber filters only. **The page renders standard `BillRowList` rows.** The fromŌåÆto transition-render idiom ŌĆö the `Ō¢Ė INTRO ŌåÆ Ō¢ĖŌ¢Ė COMMITTEE` glyph with the prior stage dimmed via a `muted` `StageIndicator`, the `Xd ago`-from-`stage_changed_at` column, the `.changes-feed` wider-stage wrapper, and `BillRow`'s `showStageTransition` opt-in ŌĆö **was removed around HO 125/148/191 and no longer exists**; `BillRow` has no `previous_stage`/transition rendering today. (This is the same idiom HO 232 found gone when it scoped the MOVERS tab.) Empty state: `No stage changes in the last 7 days.`
- `/members` ŌĆö **the merged Members + Committees two-pane browser (HO 328 ŌĆö replaced the HO 152/196/197 ranked-list-with-scatters page; the committee index folded in from the now-redirected `/committees`).** A committee rail (~312px, `getCommitteesIndex`) on the left + a member list (`1fr`) on the right. The **chamber** filter drives BOTH panes; **party/state/sort/ceremonial/search** drive the member list only. Members are still aggregated from `bills` (lineage HOs 67/89/152), now beside the rail. Filter bar (full-width strip): the `MEMBERS` title + `{total} of the 119th` count + ALL/HOUSE/SENATE `SegmentedToggle` + `PartyFilter` (R/D/I) + `StateFilter` + VOLUME/PASS RATE `SegmentedToggle` (`?sort=volume|passrate`, `getMembersRanked` ORDER BY swap) + **INCLUDE CEREMONIAL** (`CeremonialToggle`, `billsAggCte(includeCeremonial)` shifts the totals/ranking) + a member `SearchBox`. **LEFT RAIL** (`getCommitteesIndex({chamber})`): an **UPCOMING HEARINGS** group pinned at the top (`getUpcomingForRail` ŌåÆ `getUpcomingMeetings({days:7, chamber})`, soonest-per-committee, `ŌŚĘ N THIS WEEK` in the header) ŌĆö **UPCOMING, not LIVE NOW** (the schema has no in-progress / end-time signal + the page is daily-cached, so "in session now" can't be derived honestly; see oddities + the stale mock), then `CommitteeRailRow` rows (chamber tag, member count, activity bar scaled to `railMax = max(recentBillCount)`). Clicking a committee **scopes the roster**: `?committee=<systemCode>` ŌåÆ `getCommitteeRoster(code, sort, includeCeremonial)` (chair ŌåÆ ranking ŌåÆ volume order), and the per-member bar **rescales to the roster max** (vs the global filtered max unscoped). A scoped context header (`mc-ctx`) carries the committee name + `committee detail ŌåÆ` + `├Ś all members`. When a member is expanded, the rail marks the committees they sit on (lighter-amber `ŌŚÅ`, `onMarker`) and the header shows `┬Ę ŌŚÅ on N` (those that appear in the rail) via `getMemberCommittees`. **RIGHT PANE**: a topic key strip (the union of on-screen topics, most-common-first, the legend for what's rendered), the column header (`MEMBER ┬Ę BILLS┬ĘTOPIC MIX ┬Ę RATE ┬Ę ENACT ┬Ę BILLS`), then the member rows. Each row = member name + party-colored `[party-state]` bracket + `PalestineBadge` (when scored) + a **`MemberTopicBar`** (top-3 topics + `OTHR` rollup; segment widths from the member's topic counts, colors from `lib/topic-colors`; **total length scaled to `pageMax`** ŌĆö global filtered max unscoped / roster max scoped, so a bar means different things in the two states, see oddities) + RATE (green >0 / dim at 0) ┬Ę ENACT (`N Ō£ō`) ┬Ę BILLS figures. The full ranked list is **unpaginated** (`LIST_LIMIT = 600` covers all 536 current members, scrolls on overflow) so the bar scales to the true global max; scoped rosters cap at `ROSTER_CAP = 10` with the rest behind a `RosterShowAll` disclosure. Topic-mix data is `getMembersTopicMix(includeCeremonial)` ŌĆö a **flat** array (`json_each` fanout, grouped per-member in the page, cached tag `bills`, forced onto `idx_bills_sponsor_topics`). **New helpers:** `getMembersTopicMix`, `getCommitteeRoster`. **New components:** `MemberTopicBar` (server), `CommitteeRailRow` + `RosterShowAll` (client islands). The HO 152/197 `MemberProductivityScatter` pair and the HO 196 one-bar-per-sort/green-track list were **dropped** in the merge; their query `getSponsorProductivity` (+ `SponsorProductivityRow`) is **deleted (HO 328)**. Click any row to inline-expand (`?expanded=<bioguide_id>`, URL-driven single-open, `<Link replace scroll={false}>`) a `SponsorExpandedPanel` with `committeeCap={Infinity}` (uncapped COMMITTEES), fed by the 5-query `Promise.all` (`getSponsorStats` / `getSponsorTopTopics` / `getSponsorRecentBills` / `getMemberCommittees` / `getMemberAffiliations`) ŌĆö **HO 198/200 rebuilt it from the ~650px vertical stack into a ~280px 3-column card matching the HO 191 bill panel** (grid `210px ┬Ę minmax(0,1.5fr) ┬Ę minmax(0,1fr)`, `.sponsor-card-grid`/`-rail`/`-mid`/`-right`):
  - **LEFT RAIL:** 96px photo (`SponsorPhoto` via a new `width` prop ŌĆö hub stays 150px; bioguide-direct URL + `onError`ŌåÆinitials, **NOT** `depiction_url`, which the panel never had on its path) ┬Ę `Sen./Rep. First Last` identity (new `chamber` prop threaded from `MemberRanking`) + party bracket + state ┬Ę stat block (TOTAL BILLS / ENACTED n+%) ┬Ę STAGES glyph run (`--stage-*`) ┬Ę TOPICS chips ┬Ę **CAUCUSES** folded under topics (HO 152, `getMemberAffiliations`/`CaucusBadge`, skip-on-empty) ┬Ę **USCPR SCORECARD (HO 200)** ŌĆö the shared `PalestineBadge` + `total_score` + `#rank of 47` for scored members, an explicit muted **"Not scored"** for off-sheet members (the honest gap ŌĆö no fabricated/default grade; same idiom as the bill panel's "No related news"; third-party USCPR attribution mirrored from the list badge) ┬Ę stacked VIEW DETAIL / OPEN IN FEED buttons. **The state flag was dropped.**

  - **RIGHT:** COMMITTEES ┬Ę N (HO 152, `getMemberCommittees`) ŌĆö **uncapped under the HO 328 merge** (`committeeCap={Infinity}`; was ~8 on the old page) + CHAIR/RANKING badges + `Ōå│` subcommittees.
  - All three columns share ONE `--bg-row-hover` base with `border-right` dividers (the **seam fix** ŌĆö earlier per-column `--bg-panel` rails read as a color seam against the lighter middle; the HO 191 panel stays one continuous surface the same way). Caps are render-only slices; the scorecard's `total_score` is the only added column (`getMembersRanked`, existing JOIN) ŌĆö **no new queries**. URL-driven single-open via `?expanded=<bioguide_id>` (UNCHANGED; same pattern as the original HO 67 page; the `/bills` BillRowList's client-state model is the alternate idiom ŌĆö reconciling the two expand mechanisms is HO 154 normalization, not here). The spec-7 data-quality "N issues" badge stays **deferred and never built** (no schema signal) ŌĆö HO 198 confirmed there was nothing to remove.
- `/patterns` ŌĆö bill pattern visualization (HO 128; reframed HO 346ŌĆō348). **The page H1 is `LEGISLATIVE PATTERNS` (HO 346)** with a `{matched} measures in {N} forms ┬Ę out of {patternTotal} ┬Ę {pct}%` meta line (live; denominator is the page's OWN matched + unmatched, NOT the corpus BILLS TRACKED figure ŌĆö using the corpus count makes the % stop reconciling with the unmatched number) and a sans blurb ("The same forms of legislation, filed again and again. Click one to see the measures."). **Left column is `PatternBars` (HO 347, a server component ŌĆö REPLACED the deleted `PatternBubbleSVG`):** a ranked horizontal bar list, one row per regex pattern from `lib/cluster-patterns.ts`, **bar length = bill count (linear, scaled to the max)**, **bar color = % past committee on the same `--text-dim` ŌåÆ `--stage-enacted` STALLEDŌåÆMOVING ramp the bubbles used** (saturating at 30%), columns `Pattern ┬Ę [bar] ┬Ę Bills ┬Ę % past`. It **absorbed the former standalone ALL PATTERNS table** (HO 347). Selection is URL-driven via `?selected=<slug>` (validated by `sanitizeClusterId`); each row is a plain `<Link>` pushing the param with `scroll: false` (no client island), and **a pattern is ALWAYS selected** ŌĆö the page auto-selects the top (highest-count) pattern when the URL carries none, so the right column is never blank. `PatternLegend` renders the gradient strip below the bars. When selected, `PatternDrilldownPanel` renders below with a headline line `{N} bills ┬Ę {X}% past committee ┬Ę {K} enacted` ŌĆö **NOTE: the per-bill `Y% ceremonial` figure was DROPPED from this strip (HO 348)** because it contradicts the form-based filler framing (below) ŌĆö do not reintroduce it ŌĆö plus a top-5 sponsor mini-bar-chart (party-colored, name-truncated) and a `[View all N bills in feed ŌåÆ]` link to `/bills?cluster=<slug>` (HO 51 drill-out convention). Right column shows the selected pattern's top-10 most-recent bills via reused `BillRow compact` with pre-resolved `getWatchedBillIds` membership. **Filler Watch strip (HO 348, `FillerWatchStrip` ŌĆö a client island, collapsible):** sits between the meta line and the blurb. A `CEREMONIAL ┬Ę NON-BINDING` summary row (`{filed} filed ┬Ę {enacted} enacted ┬Ę {pastCommittee} past committee ┬Ę sponsors {D}%/{R}%`) that click-expands to an attrition row + a register line + a sponsor-split footer ŌĆö **every number is live-interpolated from `getFillerWatch()`** (`filed`/`pastCommittee`/`enacted`/`nonBinding`/`d`/`r`/`i`), so the prose self-reconciles each sync and can never drift. Backed by `getClusterStats()` (extended with `pastCommittee/enacted/ceremonial`), `getClusterDrilldown(clusterId)`, and `getFillerWatch()`, all `unstable_cache` tagged `bills`. **HO 199:** the top-5-sponsors sub-query `GROUP BY sponsor_bioguide_id` (was `GROUP BY sponsor_name, sponsor_party`), keeping `MAX(sponsor_name)` for the "Last, First" shape. Mobile (`< 700px`): columns stack. Internal column (`bills.cluster_id`) and helper names keep `cluster*` naming per HO 114.

  **Filler framing (the durable convention).** The cumulative ceremonial / "filler" read on `/patterns` is **form-based** ŌĆö the four ceremonial clusters (`awareness-designation`, `honoring-resolution`, `facility-naming`, `sense-of-congress`, `FILLER_WATCH_PATTERNS` in `lib/queries.ts`), with `nonBinding` = the three non-facility clusters (they cannot become law by nature; only facility namings can). This is **deliberately NOT** the per-bill `is_ceremonial` flag ŌĆö and the per-bill "% ceremonial" stat was dropped from the Patterns detail strip (HO 348) precisely because the two framings contradict each other. **Do not reintroduce a per-bill % ceremonial figure on `/patterns`.** Separately, the **dashboard `WeeklyBand` filler-share bar (HO 351) uses a BROAD definition** ŌĆö `is_ceremonial = 1 OR cluster_id IN (the four)` (`getWeeklyBandFiller`) ŌĆö so the dashboard and Patterns numbers are intentionally computed differently; that's expected, not drift.
- `/reports` ŌĆö index of weekly reports, newest first (handoff 75, redesigned HO 153). `HeaderBar` runs in `pageTitle="Weekly Reports"` + `pageCount` mode (nav + count chrome). **HO 185 removed the per-page `Reports:\>` sub-masthead** ŌĆö and with it the whole HO 154.4 `<TerminalPrompt>` / `.page-masthead` pattern that every list page (`/bills`, `/watchlist`, `/changes`, `/stale`, `/members`, `/committees`, `/patterns`, `/trends`, `/races`, `/primaries`) used to render below GroupTabs. The section name now lives once in the unified breadcrumb path (`ŌĆ”\Reports>_`), so these list pages render just `GroupTabs` + content. `.report-row` grid is `110px 1fr 70px`: amber-mono week-start date, a two-line body (`Weekly Report` title + 1-line derived lead excerpt indented under it), then a muted `read ŌåÆ` chip that lights amber-bright on hover. **HO 242 added a per-row stats strip** to the body (`ReportRow.tsx`): `Laws N ┬Ę Intro N ┬Ę Moves N` (bills enacted / non-ceremonial introductions / stage-changes that week, `tabular-nums`) ŌĆö hidden on NULL (un-backfilled) rows. **Note the deviation:** the handoff framed this as a *top* stat strip; it shipped as a **per-row** strip instead ŌĆö there's no cross-week aggregate strip above the list (the `Productivity vs. the 118th` chart is the only above-list element). Lead text is the report's first prose paragraph between the H1 and the first `##` section, markdown-noise stripped and clamped to ~180 chars via `extractReportLead(content_md)` in `lib/report-lead.ts` ŌĆö derived at read time, never stored, per spec 6 / HO 153 ("don't add a field to the generation pipeline for a display concern"). Click navigates to `/reports/[slug]`. Pagination via `?page=N` at `PAGE_SIZE = 20`. Empty state: `Reports begin Monday <next Monday>.` Backed by `getReportsWithLead(limit, offset)` (HO 242 extended it to project `laws_count`/`intro_count`/`moves_count` ŌåÆ `lawsCount`/`introCount`/`movesCount`; backfilled by `scripts/backfill-report-counts.ts`); count via `getReportCount`. - `/reports/[slug]` ŌĆö individual weekly report. - `/members/[bioguideId]` ŌĆö member hub (handoff 60, +61, +62, +77, +80). Reads from `members` + `affiliations` + `votes`/`member_votes` + `stock_trades`; refresh via `npm run sync:members`, `npm run seed:affiliations`, `npm run sync:votes`, `npm run sync:senate-votes`. HO 145 added a **Committees** section between Sponsored Bills and Voting Record, fed by `getMemberCommittees(bioguideId)`. Each row links to `/committee/[systemCode]`, shows chamber + committee type, prefixes subcommittees with `Ōå│` and an inline `┬Ę Parent` caption, and renders a `CHAIR` (amber) or `RANKING` (muted) badge when `cm.role` matches ŌĆö Vice/Co/Acting all collapse into the CHAIR badge; the raw role string lives in the row title attribute. Empty state: single muted `No committee assignments on file.` line (the assumption is every current member has at least one ŌĆö empty = freshman whose YAML hasn't been published yet, or Speaker who doesn't sit on committees by tradition; both worth surfacing).

- `/committee/[systemCode]` ŌĆö committee detail (HO 144 + HO 146). Header card: name, chamber, type, parent-committee link if `parent_system_code IS NOT NULL`, subcommittees roster (flat ŌĆö no nesting in v1), retired badge if `is_current = 0`. HO 146 added a two-chart strip between the header card and the members/recent-bills grid: **`CommitteeActivityChart`** (left, ~60%) ŌĆö stacked monthly bars over the current Congress, bars segmented by 4-bucket `activity_type` collapse (Referred/Markup/Reported/Other), throughput-funnel color mapping (`--stage-committee` ŌåÆ `--stage-floor` ŌåÆ `--stage-enacted` ŌåÆ `--text-dim`); legend chips only render for buckets present in the data; renders muted `Not enough activity to chart.` when the committee has fewer than 5 activity rows; SVG idiom forked from `BillsTimeSeries` (`CHART_HEIGHT=240`, `VB_WIDTH=1000`, same `PAD`, same `SvgGridY` + `SvgLegend`). **`CommitteeTopicDistribution`** (right, ~40%) ŌĆö single-column horizontal bars, topic colors from `lib/topic-colors`, top-8 + Other rollup, reuses the `.topic-chamber-row` grid styling from `TopicMixByChamber`; renders muted `Topic data sparse for this committee.` when total non-ceremonial topic-tagged bills < 5. Both feed off the HO 146 helpers (`getCommitteeActivityByPeriod`, `getCommitteeTopicMix`) ŌĆö see the helpers entry for the `LOWER()` normalization that handles the `committee_bills.activity_type` case-duplicate. Hearings/meetings, subcommittee rollup grouping, and hover tooltips are explicitly out of scope (deferred). Two body sections side-by-side on desktop (`md:grid-cols-[2fr_3fr]`), stacked on mobile: **Members** (left, ~40%) and **Recent activity** (right, ~60%). Members are reordered in TS to majority ŌåÆ minority ŌåÆ unside; within each block the row order already comes off `getCommitteeMembers` as `party_side ASC, rank ASC NULLS LAST` so chair/ranking float to the top. Chair/ranking rows render in `--accent-amber`; everyone else in `--text-primary`. Recent bills come from `getCommitteeBills(systemCode, 25, 30)` ŌĆö the helper now takes an optional `sinceDays` arg and returns `CommitteeBillRow[]` (`{ bill: FeedBill; activityType; activityDate }`) so the page can show the per-committee activity caption (`Referred to ┬Ę 3d ago`, computed via `daysSince`) immediately above each `BillRow` rather than the global `latest_action_*` line the row already carries. Each bill is rendered as **two sibling `<li>` elements** under the section's `<ul>`: an `ActivityCaption` muted-uppercase line first, then a compact `BillRow`. Two-li-per-row is HTML-valid (the `ul` content model is "zero or more li"). `BillRow` is used `compact` with the page-resolved `watchedSet` so the star renders correctly without a per-row fetch. Empty states for both sections are single muted lines, not full empty chrome (a quiet committee like `hspw12` Highways and Transit shows "No bills with committee activity in the last 30 days."). Unknown `systemCode` renders a friendly empty state with a back link, not `notFound()`. Cached at the query layer under tag `committees`.
- `/race/[id]` ŌĆö race hub (handoff 62). Race name + cycle + days-to-election countdown. Rating block (Sabato seven, party-colored chip) when hand-curated. Incumbent card linking to `/members/<bioguide_id>` (or "OPEN SEAT" placeholder when `incumbent_bioguide_id` is null). Candidate roster from `race_candidates`, ordered won_primary ŌåÆ running ŌåÆ declared ŌåÆ withdrew ŌåÆ name; withdrawn rows render dimmed. Stub state (no rating, no candidates) shows a single muted "Incumbent running for re-election. No competitive rating yet." line. Source URL + `last_verified` date at the bottom. Unknown id renders a friendly empty state, not Next's `notFound()`. Reads from `races` + `race_candidates` + (incumbent) `members`. ID format: `<STATE>-<DD>-<YYYY>` for House (zero-padded district), `S-<STATE>-<YYYY>` for Senate ŌĆö produced by `lib/race-id.ts::raceIdFromMember`.

Empty rosters show muted "roster pending". **Ōśģ = advancer (the HO 207 reframe):** Ōśģ marks every candidate who **won / advanced** (`status='winner'`) ŌĆö runoffs advance two, so **two Ōśģs is valid and expected** (TX-Sen R = Cornyn 42% + Paxton 40.5% both Ōśģ; `backfill:primary-results` writes `status` alongside `vote_pct`). The **seat incumbent** is a *separate* cue (amber name in the fallback list, an `INC` badge in the expand) so it never collides with Ōśģ on one glyph. It's still resolved via the `seat_incumbent_bioguide` subquery in `PRIMARY_SELECT` (current House officeholder matched by `state`+`district`, `is_current`; falls back to the raw `incumbent` flag where unresolved ŌĆö at-large/senate/open, Ōēż1 there), which drives the `INC` badge + the `/members/[bioguideId]` links, **not** Ōśģ. That subquery beats `races.incumbent_bioguide_id` (whose `primaries.race_id` link is dead 3/907, with cycle gaps + at-large excluded). The raw `primary_candidates.incumbent` flag ("is a sitting member of Congress") still drives the member link and legitimately flags >1 candidate in top-two/redraw contests (CA-40: Calvert+Kim; TX-18: Menefee+Green). **HO 148 click-to-expand, single-open** via a shared `PrimaryExpandProvider` context (client-side ŌĆö wraps the whole list so it survives any native collapse): full candidate field with per-candidate **share % + advancer Ōśģ + `INC` badge + `/members/[bioguideId]` links** (NO photos ŌĆö separate future decision). The share bar was specced at HO 203, deferred while `vote_pct` was 100% NULL, unblocked by HO 206, and **shipped at HO 207** (results share, not polling ŌĆö no polling model exists). **Voted-block guard (HO 208):** past contests with no roster AND no result are hidden from the voted block ŌĆö a DISPLAY guard over two unfixed data problems (see the primaries data-debt note under "Things to watch for"); the clean page is **not** clean data. Reads `primaries` + `primary_candidates` (see "Runoff tracking" + the primaries cron notes). **Map-first as of HO 210:** the same `geoAlbersUsa` `CartogramShell` (PRIMARIES variant ŌĆö VOTED/SOON/LATER recency bands) renders above this list as the default view, the date-sorted list one MAP/LIST toggle away; the pinned state card reuses the HO 207 `ShareBar` for voted contests and a `SCHEDULED ┬Ę <full date>` list for unvoted.
