The shared shell, server-only geometry (`lib/us-map-geo.ts`), the two-coloring DO-NOT-UNIFY discipline, and the SOON rolling-window + VOTED-precedence are all documented under the `/races` entry. **District modal (HO 226 ŌĆö sibling of the HO 225 Races modal):** `/primaries` wraps `CartogramShell` in **`PrimariesMap`** (mirror of `RacesMap`) holding modal state + the month scrubber; reuses the HO 225 `onStatePick` prop. **Three minimal, variant-scoped CartogramShell touches** (all behind `variant==="primaries"` / the optional `dimmedStates` prop so a `/races` render hits none ŌĆö verified: races map renders 0 `opacity` attrs, purple fills, no `ŌŚÅ` labels): (1) `primariesFill` recolored to deeper recency bands `VOTED #0e7490 / SOON #b45309 / LATER #1e2740 / NONE #11161f`; (2) a `ŌŚÅ N` badge in the state label for multi-primary states (`cell.count` = contest count, set in `buildPrimariesCartogram`); (3) the optional `dimmedStates` prop dims states outside the scrubber month (opacity 0.28). **Month scrubber** (`PrimaryScrubber`, exported from `PrimaryDistrictModal`) = static segments `MAR┬ĘJUN┬ĘAUG┬ĘSEP┬ĘALL`, no motion; `PrimariesMap` derives each state's month from its MAX `primary_date` and dims the rest. **`PrimaryDistrictModal`** reuses the HO 225 shell (`.rdm-*`) + the cached `/api/races/district-geo/[state]` route (geometry is chamber-agnostic, shared with Races); pick chips + map districts are keyed by `raceId` = the district seatId (`{ST}-{DD}-2026` house / `S-{ST}-2026` senate, set on each primaries `CartogramContest` so a polygon groups its D + R primaries). Map fills are **recency only** (voted teal / upcoming amber / none recede) ŌĆö NOT results-colored (HO 205 verdict; a later layer). **`PrimaryDistrictCard`** = **two party columns** (D primary | R primary; one for single/open), each in one of three RESULTS-era states (supersedes spec-4's dead polling card): **VOTED+DECIDED** (extracted `ShareBar`, 1 Ōśģ, `WON ┬Ę advances to Nov`) / **VOTED+RUNOFF** (`ShareBar`, **two Ōśģs**, amber `RUNOFF ┬Ę top 2 advance <date>` ŌĆö e.g. TX-Sen R Cornyn 42 + Paxton 40.5) / **NOT-YET-VOTED** (no bar, `SCHEDULED ┬Ę votes <date>` + incumbent-first roster, `no results yet ┬Ę N filed`). Columns **bottom-align via a flex `col-spacer`** that pushes the status footer flush (replaces the deferred news-pin ŌĆö there is NO news block, no portrait, no front-runner/polling framing). Export = client-side markdown of the field(s), `{district}-primary-report.md`, **no news section**. Mobile `<700` deferred (falls back to the single list).
- `/electoral` ŌĆö the **consolidated Electoral surface (HO 333 ŌĆö moved from `/races`; Races + Primaries collapsed into ONE surface)**, **map-first** (HOs 62/71/72/210; LIST redesigned HO 222). **The competitive map on top + a NEW primary-calendar timeline band below it**, wired so the timeline drives an amber highlight on the map. **Stack:** `HeaderBar(basePath="/electoral") ŌåÆ <h1> ŌåÆ <p> ŌåÆ RacesHeroBand ŌåÆ ElectoralBoard`. **No GroupTabs** ŌĆö the `races`/electoral sub-nav group (Races ┬Ę Primaries, HO 173) is **retired** (collapsed to a single member; the page renders no strip). `/races` + `/primaries` **308-redirect here** (`permanentRedirect`); the nav item is relabeled **Electoral** (key still `"races"`); breadcrumb reads `ŌĆ”\119TH\Electoral>`. **`ElectoralBoard`** (client, HO 333) owns the shared `locked`(dates) / `hovered` / `openAbbr`(modal) state and renders `CartogramShell` (highlight props) + `RaceDistrictModal` + `PrimaryTimeline` + the readout. **Timeline ŌåÆ map highlight (the new interaction):** click a `PrimaryTimeline` bar ŌåÆ that date's states paint amber (`--accent-amber-bright`, label flipped to `--bg-base`) on the map; selections **accumulate** across dates (drop one by re-clicking its bar; CLEAR ALL empties); hover a bar ŌåÆ transient amber **outline** preview of that date's states. Non-highlighted states keep their purple competitive fill (**no dimming**), static (no transitions). **Highlighted states are a readout ŌĆö clicking an amber state does nothing ŌĆö but clicking ANY state still opens the HO 225 district modal** (Corey's call, HO 333: state-click drill KEPT, a deliberate deviation from the handoff's "read-only map" ŌĆö the district drill + metro panels HO 236/237 are preserved). **The timeline is Sen+House COMBINED per date** (bar height = total contests; the hero band already separates House/Senate *control*). Data: **`getPrimaryCalendar(2026)`** (`lib/queries.ts`, **uncached plain `db.execute`** ŌĆö no primaries cache tag exists, matches `getDashboardPrimaries`; returns `{date, states[], contestCount}` one row/date, PAST + future, sorted asc). VOTED (cyan `#0e7490`, date Ōēż today) vs UPCOMING (amber `#b45309`) is a render-time compare in `PrimaryTimeline` (hand-rolled SVG ŌĆö only `d3-geo`/`d3-hierarchy` installed, so no `d3-scale`; matches the `BillsIntroTimeline` idiom). `DISPLAY_STALE_STATES` is carried (the map is the existing competitive map, byte-identical purple base ŌĆö highlight is an additive amber layer). **The HO 226 primaries recency-map + its district modal/scrubber are superseded by the timeline** (`PrimariesMap`/`PrimaryDistrictModal`/`RacesMap` left unreferenced ŌĆö backlog open loop). **A literal `geoAlbersUsa` US choropleth (`CartogramShell`, client) is the DEFAULT view; the LIST is one MAP/LIST toggle away.** A tile-grid cartogram built earlier in HO 210 was **rejected in design** ("squares are lifeless, don't read as 'my state' ŌĆö geographic legibility won") and replaced by the literal map ŌĆö **do NOT re-optimize back to squares.** (Historical: `/races` was the pre-HO-333 route name; `/primaries` mounted the same `CartogramShell` with the PRIMARIES variant.)
  - **LIST view (`components/RaceListView.tsx`, HO 222 ŌĆö replaced the old 5-column rating matrix `RaceRow`/`RaceSection`/`.race-row`):** a consensus-led, toss-ups-first row list, client island for the HO 148 single-open accordion (**NOT** the bill panel-fetch path ŌĆö every field rides on `RaceIndexRow`, zero lazy fetch). Fed `senate`/`house` `RaceIndexRow[]` through `listSlot`. **Row LŌåÆR:** 3px severity rail (amber-bright toss / amber lean / dim likely-solid by `|consensusScore|`) ┬Ę seat ID ┬Ę incumbent + `[party]` (HO 221 OPEN treatment when `incumbentRunning===0`: `ŌŚŗ` glyph + amber `OPEN` pill + dim `(retiring)` name; `OPEN SEAT` when `incumbentName` null) ┬Ę consensus chip (1px ratingBorderColor) ┬Ę 3-segment Cook┬ĘSabato┬ĘInside `SpreadBar` (each colored by that rater's rating; **missing rater = `--bg-base` empty slot**) ┬Ę `ŌŚå` divergence flag (Kalshi favored party vs consensus direction; amber when they disagree, transparent otherwise) ┬Ę 2024 House `MarginBar` (Senate ŌåÆ `ŌĆö senate`, House-null ŌåÆ `ŌĆö no data`) ┬Ę incumbent cash (plain `--text-secondary`). **Expand:** per-rater detail spelled out + `KalshiLine` + Race-hub link. **Summary readout** above the rows: `137 ┬Ę 24 toss-up ┬Ę 37 lean ┬Ę 76 likely/solid ┬Ę ŌŚå 4 markets disagree with raters` (live reduce over the rows). **Two DROPPED premises (HO 222 Phase 1, flawed in the handoff):** (1) the `ŌŚÅ N` **news flag** + the expand's NEWS-MAPPED block + the state breaking strip ŌĆö **there is NO raceŌåÆnews linkage** (`news_mentions` is bill-keyed; a race has no bills; building one is out of scope) ŌåÆ degrade to neutral, not faked; (2) the strength-distinct chip/spread palette (Likely #93c5fd / Solid #1e3a8a) ŌĆö **NOT used**, it contradicts the live `RatingChip` "no strength tint axis" convention + "existing tokens only"; the LIST uses the **lean-only** palette. **CHECK 2 (cash threshold):** the toss-up+lean cash distribution showed **no natural break** (House rises smoothly $0ŌåÆ$10.8M; Senate n=6, ~10├Ś scale), so cash is plain `--text-secondary` everywhere ŌĆö **no amber "thin" cutoff** (`scripts/diagnostic/cash-dist-222.ts`). **Shared helpers (HO 222):** `ratingColor`/`ratingBorderColor`/`partyColor`/`partyWord`/`surname`/`nameKey`/`resolveKalshiFavoriteParty`/`kalshiDivergesFromConsensus` live in **`lib/race-colors.ts`**; the presentational `MarginBar`/`KalshiLine`/`SpreadBar`/`formatCash` cells in **`components/race-cells.tsx`** ŌĆö both `RaceMapCard` (MAP card) AND `RaceListView` (LIST) import them, and `RatingChip` now sources its color from `lib/race-colors` too, so the three rating surfaces render from ONE source. Helpers take **primitive args** (rating string, signed score, KalshiOdds, `{name,party}` roster) ŌĆö NOT a whole `CartogramContest`/`RaceIndexRow`; each surface maps its fields at the call site.
  - **Geometry ŌĆö `lib/us-map-geo.ts` is SERVER-ONLY:** it statically imports the ~1 MB `us-atlas@3` states-10m topology + `d3-geo`/`topojson-client` and emits a serializable `{viewBox, states:[{abbr,d,cx,cy}], leaderLabels}` payload, keeping all of that **off the client bundle** (the client renders plain `<path>`/`<text>`). us-atlas states-10m ships **unprojected lat/long**, so it applies `geoAlbersUsa().fitSize([975,610])` ŌĆö NOT a null projection (some us-atlas builds are pre-projected; this one isn't ŌĆö verified by probe). Territories (PR/GU/AS/VI/MP) project to null under albersUsa and drop cleanly. **Name-join (the one map-form gotcha):** the topology keys on the FULL state name (`properties.name` = "Pennsylvania"/"District of Columbia"); cells key on the 2-letter abbr ŌĆö bridged via `STATE_NAME_TO_ABBR` (`lib/states.ts`). DC has no visible polygon at this zoom ŌåÆ fixed small marker. Small NE/mid-Atlantic states (VT/NH/MA/RI/CT/NJ/DE/MD/DC) get **leader-line labels** in a right-edge gutter; the stack **hugs the latitude cluster** (not the full map height ŌĆö else DC stranded 310px below its origin) and is ordered northŌåÆsouth so lines never cross. Peek cards are **pixel-clamped to the map area** so they never cover the gutter or run off-screen (flip left near the right edge).
  - **Coloring ŌĆö TWO SEPARATE functions, DO NOT UNIFY** (`racesFill`/`primariesFill` in `CartogramShell`; never merge into one parameterized colorer): RACES = **purple ramp by competitive-race COUNT** (magnitude, not lean: `0 #1a2030 / 1 #3b3585 / 2 #5048b0 / 3 #6a60d0 / 4+ #8b82e8`, brightened so the 27 count-1 states read against the base; count is hover-revealed as `PA 4`, lean is NOT on the fill). PRIMARIES = **recency hues** VOTED `#06b6d4` / SOON `#fbbf24` / LATER `#2a3344`. **Palette discipline:** purple = races-magnitude THIS SURFACE ONLY; amber = urgency app-wide (cursor / floor stage / active filter, and here primaries SOON) ŌĆö deliberately NOT reused for races heat; cyan = primaries VOTED. The two tabs never share a meaningful color; legends are self-contained; you never see both at once.
  - **Competitive-count predicate (the one that bit us ŌĆö name both, never swap):** the RACES tile count is the **`getRacesIndex(2026)` per-state row count** = "any race with Ōēź1 seeded `race_ratings` row for the cycle" (**INNER JOIN existence ŌåÆ 137 races / 44 states**), so map count == LIST length by construction. This is **NOT** `ABS(rating_score)<=1` ŌĆö that cut belongs to **`getMostCompetitiveRaces`** (the dashboard `CompetitiveRacesBlock`), a DIFFERENT query yielding **61**. A future sweep MUST NOT substitute one for the other. (Prose drift to ignore: 21 of the 137 are all-Solid consensus, so the page's "anything other than Solid/Safe" copy doesn't perfectly match its own behavior ŌĆö row-counting `getRacesIndex` sidesteps it.)
  - **PRIMARIES bands ŌĆö SOON definition + VOTED precedence:** SOON = the **next 4 distinct FUTURE state-uniform primary dates** (`MAX(primary_date) GROUP BY state`), **rolling ŌĆö NOT a fixed 30-day window** (that goes dark in the AugŌĆōSep gap); ties share a date. **VOTED takes precedence over SOON**, and the window is computed over not-yet-voted states only ŌĆö so LA (voted in May, with a June runoff date its `MAX` would otherwise catch) renders VOTED, and the window rolls to the next not-voted date to keep 4. LATER = everything else; inactive = no primary (DC). Today: 22 VOTED / 9 SOON / 19 LATER / 1 inactive.
  - **Pinned card (BASIC + null-safe, HO 210 Pass 2; `RaceMapCard` / `PrimaryMapCard`):** RACES = **Senate-first** click-to-expand accordion (single-open) ŌĆö collapsed: incumbent face (`incumbent_depiction_url`, `onError`ŌåÆinitials; **137/137 rated incumbents have a photo and a resolved name ŌĆö a blank row would be a bug, not data**) ┬Ę `[party] SEAT ┬Ę name` ┬Ę consensus rating; expanded: incumbent (ŌåÆ member page) **+ incumbent CASH-on-hand mini-metric (HO 212; `.racecard-cash`, right-aligned on the incumbent row)** + challenger rows **or** a "Challenger field not yet available" placeholder + Race hub link. **Challenger names (HO 213 Part A)** are harvested DB-to-DB from `primary_candidates` winners (`status='winner'`) into `race_candidates` by `npm run backfill:race-challengers` ŌĆö the non-incumbent primary advancer(s) for each rated seat, joined `state`+`chamber`+`district` (`CAST(p.district AS INTEGER)`), excluding the seat's own incumbent (`pc.bioguide_id <> r.incumbent_bioguide_id`; the HO 213 probe found **0** incumbent winners with a NULL bioguide, so bioguide-exclude is sufficient). Written `status='won_primary'`, `source_url='harvest:primary_winner'` (a **sentinel** ŌĆö the backfill deletes+re-derives only sentinel rows and **skips any race that already carries a non-sentinel/curated row**, so the HO 171/174/182 hand-seeded strip rosters (NJ-07/PA-10/S-GA/S-ME, with their `withdrew`/`running` nuance) are never clobbered). **Coverage is partial by design: 53 newly-filled + 4 hand-seeded = 57/137**; the rest keep the null-safe placeholder (only voted+rostered primaries yield a winner). Runoff/top-two seats legitimately get 2ŌĆō4 advancer rows. **No challenger photo** (HO 211: blocked, no source ŌĆö placeholder only, never attempted). Re-run after new primaries resolve; flush with `POST /api/revalidate?tag=races`. **Incumbent cash** is `member_fundraising.cash_on_hand` (FEC, HO 83) joined 1:1 on `(bioguide_id, cycle)` in `getRacesIndex` ŌåÆ `RaceIndexRow.incumbentCashOnHand` (**CENTS**; rendered via `formatDollarsCompact`). **93% coverage (128/137)**; **null = no filing on record ŌåÆ field omitted cleanly; a real filed-empty `0` renders `$0`** (0ŌēĀnull, same render-the-gap-honestly discipline as primaries `vote_pct`). **Incumbent-only ŌĆö challenger cash is structurally unavailable** (table is bioguide-keyed; challengers have no bioguide). The HO 212 placement defaulted to the expanded row because the referenced design mock (`style3-expandable-news.html`) **was never in the repo** ŌĆö collapsed row stays tight (face/seat/name/rating). **OPEN-seat tag (HO 221, shipped)** ŌĆö when a rated seat's incumbent isn't running (`races.incumbent_running = 0`, hand-seeded from Ballotpedia's not-running list via `races-seed.json` ŌåÆ `RaceIndexRow.incumbentRunning` ŌåÆ `CartogramContest.isOpen`), the **collapsed row** swaps the `[party]` chip for a dim `ŌŚŗ`, adds an amber `OPEN` pill (`.racecard-open-tag`; **amber = attention, NOT purple/cyan**), and shows the departing incumbent **dimmed with a `(retiring)` cue** (no fabricated successor ŌĆö `race_candidates` still carries any challengers); the **expand** relabels them `┬Ę retiring` and **suppresses the cash line** (no incumbent-cash story on an open seat). **NULL is NOT open** ŌĆö only an explicit `0` lights the tag; uncurated seats render as normal defended incumbents (the honest default). **This is a NEW signal, distinct from `incumbent_bioguide_id IS NULL`** (vacancy/unmapped, 0 cases ŌĆö can't express a retirement; the CHECK-1 diagnostic). **34 OPEN tags today** (9 Senate + 25 House), hand-curated/quarterly. **`S-OK` is deliberately held out** ŌĆö its incumbent is miscoded (shows Lankford/Class-III; the 2026 OK seat is the Class-II Mullin seat, now an appointee barred from running), a member-data fix tracked in `docs/backlog.md`, not tagged until fixed. **2024 House margin bar (HO 214, shipped)** renders at the result-bar insertion point on House rows: `races.margin_2024` (REAL, **SIGNED pct points ŌĆö R-won positive, D-won negative**, the `race_ratings.score` convention) ŌåÆ `RaceIndexRow.margin2024` ŌåÆ `MarginBar` (`.racecard-margin`: `2024` tag + magnitude-scaled party-colored track + `R+14.2`/`D+2.7`/`EVEN` label; **EVEN only when `|m|<0.1`** so a razor 0.2-pt win still shows its winner). **House-only by design** ŌĆö Senate rows render NO bar (no 2024 general; null-safe absence, like HO 212 cash on uncovered seats). Backfilled by `npm run backfill:2024-margin` (`scripts/backfill-2024-margin.ts`): **106/108 House index seats**; honest gaps **ME-02 (RCV ŌĆö no standard votebox)** + **TX-09 (uncontested, Al Green 100%, `lt2`)**, **0 unresolved/404**. **Source + isolation (the HO 206 wrong-votebox trap, locked):** the 2024 general is on the SEPARATE per-seat 2024 page (`/State's_Nth_ŌĆ”election,_2024`), NOT the cached 2026 page (which carries only 2026 voteboxes + a 2024-*presidential*-by-district section ŌĆö a different metric). **URL resolution** harvests the canonical 2024 link from the cached 2026 page (ground truth ŌĆö handles the possessive variance that 404'd a templated `Texas%27s_15th`: the real link is `Texas%27_15th`; all 435 cached pages carry the link), template fallback. **Votebox isolation** scopes to the page's main `Candidates_and_election_results` section (the page's "General election for U.S. House" voteboxes ALSO appear under `District_history` as the 2018/2020/2022 generals ŌĆö a page-wide header match pulls those; the section scope + a 2024-date guard drop them), then reads the results_table shares; party per row via bar-color class ŌåÆ fusion `(D / ŌĆ”)` suffix ŌåÆ thumbnail wrapper; winner = highest share. **Correction to the HO 213 probe note:** it claimed ME-02 "cleanly isolates the 2024 general (Golden vs Theriault)" ŌĆö wrong; those `General election` voteboxes on ME-02 are the *historical* (2018+) generals, and ME-02's actual 2024 result is RCV with no standard votebox (hence its honest gap). **Live fetch needs a browser UA** (curl/WebFetch get a ~51KB bot stub; `node fetch` + UA works); 2024 pages are uncached, ~108 polite live fetches; idempotent. Flush with `POST /api/revalidate?tag=races`. PRIMARIES = VOTED ŌåÆ the HO 207 `ShareBar` (**extracted to `components/ShareBar.tsx` in HO 226** ŌĆö was inline in `PrimaryRow`; props-only `{cands,tint}`, reused as-is by three surfaces now: the single-list `PrimaryRow`, `PrimaryMapCard`, and the HO 226 `PrimaryDistrictCard`) / UNVOTED ŌåÆ `SCHEDULED ┬Ę <full date>` + incumbent-first field list. **Per-seat Kalshi odds (HO 218, shipped)** render a `KALSHI ┬Ę {favorite} {NN}%` line at the insertion point right after `MarginBar` (`.racecard-kalshi`: neutral `KALSHI` tag + `┬Ę` + party-colored favorite). Source is Kalshi's **public/no-auth** API (`external-api.kalshi.com/trade-api/v2`, HO 217). A **GitHub-Actions cron** (`/api/cron/kalshi`, `.github/workflows/kalshi-tick.yml`, every 2h ŌĆö Hobby caps Vercel cron at daily and odds move intraday; the route's full-feed scan ran 16.4s end-to-end, well under the 55s soft timeout) scans the **open-events feed** (`events?status=open&with_nested_markets=true&limit=200`, ~37 pages, 250ms throttle ŌĆö the `series_ticker` filter is unreliable and the `markets` feed is too large to page; events `limit` caps at 200), parses each `-26` event ticker to our raceId, keeps the **favored outcome** (max `last_price_dollars`), and batch-upserts `kalshi_odds` (one row per race_id; loose-linked, writes ~469 seats incl. unrated ones; `getRacesIndex` LEFT JOIN 1:1 picks the 137 ŌåÆ `RaceIndexRow.kalshiOdds` ŌåÆ `CartogramContest.kalshiOdds`). **Ticker parse (locked HO 218 Phase 1 ŌĆö `lib/kalshi.ts::tickerToRaceId`):** House tries FOUR schemes in order ŌĆö `KXHOUSERACE-{ST}{DD}-26` | `HOUSEPARTY-{ST}{DD}-26` | `KXHOUSE{ST}{DD}-26` | `HOUSE{ST}{D}-26` ŌåÆ `{ST}-{pad2 DD}-2026`. **The competitive seats live on the bare `HOUSE{ST}{D}` scheme, NOT `KXHOUSERACE` ŌĆö the handoff's single-scheme rule was STALE; `KXHOUSERACE`-only covers safe seats and silently dropped all 60 competitive House seats (Phase 1 caught this: 49/108 ŌåÆ 108/108).** Senate: `SENATE(FL|OH)S-26` specials + `(KX)?SENATE{ST}-26(NOV)?` ŌåÆ `S-{ST}-2026` (no per-state LA hardcode; the optional `NOV` covers LA). Strict anchoring self-rejects primaries (`KXSENATE{ST}{D|R}-26`) + derivative markets (MOV/ADVANCE/SEATS/CONTROL/TURNOUT). **Render ŌĆö named favorite with a party degrade (`RaceMapCard::KalshiLine`):** `favorite_is_party` (a bare party string ŌĆö **~65% of matched markets, the majority/first-class path**) ŌåÆ party-colored `Dem`/`Rep`/`Ind` from `favorite_party`; a candidate-name market shows the surname, party resolved against the card's **own roster** (incumbent + challengers) for color, else neutral `--text-secondary` ŌĆö **never fabricate a party the API didn't give.** Null odds (no Kalshi general market) OR a market past `close_time` ŌåÆ render nothing (null-safe absence, like cash/margin). **Coverage 136/137** ŌĆö only `S-KY` lacks a general market (KY runs only D/R primary markets; null-safe placeholder). The cron `revalidateTag("races")`s; manual flush `POST /api/revalidate?tag=races`. Diagnostic: `scripts/diagnostic/kalshi-218.ts` (the Phase 1 cross-join). **Chamber-control hero band (HO 219, shipped ŌĆö closes the chamber-control thread):** NOT part of the card ŌĆö a 3-cell page-level stat row (`components/RacesHeroBand.tsx`, `.races-hero-band`) at the top of `/races`, **between the `<p>` description and `CartogramShell`**: HOUSE CONTROL ┬Ę SENATE CONTROL ┬Ę SEATS IN PLAY. Control odds come from Kalshi's two FIXED events `CONTROLH-2026` / `CONTROLS-2026` (each a D + R outcome market) via `lib/kalshi.ts::fetchChamberControl` (two direct event reads ŌĆö no scanning) on the **same HO 218 2h GitHub-Actions cron** (`/api/cron/kalshi`); **BOTH exact pcts are stored** ŌĆö the two `last_price_dollars` sum to ~99ŌĆō101, NOT 100, so the loser is never `100ŌłÆfav` ŌĆö as ONE `dashboard_state` JSON blob (`key='kalshi_chamber_control'`), read by `getChamberControl()` (`unstable_cache` tag `races`; null-safe per chamber ŌåÆ cell shows `ŌĆö`). Render is **data-driven**: the higher pct is favored (letter+pct in its `--party-*` color), the loser trails `--text-dim`; a market flip re-colors for free. One amber `LIVE` pill on the HOUSE cell only (the band's single liveness signal ŌĆö **no timestamp**, decided against). **SEATS IN PLAY count = `getRacesIndex` (137 rated ┬Ę 29 SEN ┬Ę 108 HOUSE), already in hand on the page ŌĆö NOT `getMostCompetitiveRaces` (61); the predicate-trap that broke HO 210, name both never swap.** **No `/ 469 up` denominator** (decided against ŌĆö no source). **RACES-route-only:** `/races` and `/primaries` are SEPARATE routes, so the band is simply not mounted on `/primaries` (no tab conditional ŌĆö supersedes the handoff's active-tab-signal framing). **Card boundary:** cash (HO 212) + challenger names (HO 213) + 2024 House margin (HO 214) + per-seat Kalshi odds (HO 218) all shipped ŌĆö the expanded House card is fully populated (Senate shows cash + Kalshi) ŌĆö and the **chamber-control hero stat (HO 219) now ships at the page level**; everything still richer ŌĆö rater spread, the **rating trend sparkline (its change-detect logging is now LIVE ŌĆö HO 220; the `rating_history` series accumulates from 2026-06, so the chart is the remaining build once weeks of data exist ŌĆö no longer "needs logging started first")**, news-to-seat, BREAKING strip ŌĆö is the SEPARATE **rich-card arcs**; `RaceMapCard` leaves documented null-safe insertion points.
  - **Data plumbing:** cells are built by `lib/cartogram-data.ts` (`buildRacesCartogram` / `buildPrimariesCartogram`, pure ŌĆö no DB). `getRacesIndex` projects `incumbent_depiction_url` (members JOIN) + **`incumbent_cash_on_hand` (member_fundraising LEFT JOIN, 1:1 on bioguide+cycle ŌĆö does NOT multiply the 137 rows, HO 212)** + the per-seat `kalshiOdds` (kalshi_odds LEFT JOIN, HO 218) + **`polymarketOdds` (polymarket_odds LEFT JOIN, HO 260 ŌĆö Senate-only, feeds the v2 rich card's ŌŚå diamond + POLYMARKET cell)** + consensus rating onto `RaceIndexRow`; **HO 225 added `incumbentFirstElected`** (min `startYear` from the members JOIN's `terms_json`, parsed in `firstElectedFromTerms` ŌĆö drives the modal card's tenure / FIRST ELECTED). `buildRacesCartogram` now also projects `raceId` + `incumbentFirstElected` + `raterSpread {cook,sabato,ie}` onto each `CartogramContest` (the modal needs the per-rater strings ŌĆö consensus alone can't drive the spread bar). `getRaceCandidatesForCycle(cycle)` returns a **flat array** (grouped in the builder ŌĆö a `Map` would round-trip to `{}` through `unstable_cache`'s JSON serialization); the raw `PrimaryWithCandidates` rides on each primaries contest for the ShareBar.
  - **District modal (HO 225 ŌĆö the click-into-a-state interaction, FIRST consumer of `lib/district-geo.ts`):** clicking a state on the `/races` MAP opens a centered modal (state district-overview map + pick chips + incumbent-anchored detail card). **CartogramShell additive-handler pattern:** CartogramShell gained ONE optional prop `onStatePick?(abbr)`; when present the active-state `onClick` calls it instead of `setPinned` (the inline `.cart-report`). **`/races` wraps CartogramShell in `RacesMap`** (new client) which holds modal open-state and passes `onStatePick`; **`/primaries` renders CartogramShell directly with no `onStatePick`, so its pinŌåÆinline behavior is unchanged** (HO 226 builds the primaries modal). Hover popover untouched (only `onClick` changed ŌĆö verified by diff). **Geometry over the client/server boundary:** `getStateDistrictGeometry` is server-only, so the modal fetches per-state path strings from **`GET /api/races/district-geo/[state]`** on open (lazy, matches `/api/bill/[id]/panel`). That route is **`unstable_cache`-wrapped** (`revalidate` 30d, tag `district-geo`) ŌĆö the geometry is static per state, must project ONCE not on every open. The response carries a server-resolved **`seatId` per polygon**, so the client never imports the server-only join helpers ŌĆö it matches `seatId` against the state's contests for clickability + highlight (pick chip Ōåö map both key off `seatId`/`raceId`). **`RaceDistrictModal`** (client): header `CALIFORNIA ┬Ę 7 COMPETITIVE OF 52`, maps band (competitive districts filled via `race-colors` `ratingColor`, non-competitive recede `#1c2433`; click ŌåÆ amber outline), pick-chip row (House + Senate; Senate chips are card-only, no polygon), `Ōåō EXPORT REPORT` (client-side markdown from card data, **no news section**) + `RACE HUB ŌåÆ` (dimmed until selected), detail panel. **`RaceDistrictCard`** (client): incumbent-anchored, **three cases** picking render from what's present ŌĆö Case 1 incumbent-only (Ōēł default, rich profile + "no challenger on file" line), Case 2 incumbent + challenger row(s) (NOW Ōēł58 seats, not the handoff's stale "4" ŌĆö HO 213 harvested primary winners into `race_candidates`; both the HO 213-harvested and the HO 171/174 hand-seeded paths render the same row), Case 3 open seat (`incumbentRunning===0`, "OPEN SEAT ┬Ę NO INCUMBENT" + lean explainer + 2024 result + field-timing, candidates as `CANDIDATE` rows with no INCUMBENT tag). NEVER reserves space it can't fill (no VS layout). Reuses the `RaceMapCard` incumbent idiom + HO 222 `race-colors`/`race-cells`. **Minimal modal shell** (`.rdm-*` in globals.css) ŌĆö built from existing tokens + the `.cart-report` amber/close idiom because **no reusable drawer exists** (HO 132.1/166/170 drawers were retired). **Metro-zoom panels (HO 236) + leader-lines (HO 237) ŌĆö SHIPPED** (no longer the deferred "cramped-but-functional at overview" state): dense states get up to **2 inset sub-map panels** (`METRO_PANELS` in `lib/metro-panels.ts`, a hand-curated per-state `{label, districtIds}` list ŌĆö CA = SOUTHERN CALIFORNIA `40/45` + CENTRAL CALIFORNIA `06/13/21`; **cap = 2 panels/state**). Each inset subset-renders its districts at its OWN `geoAlbers().fitExtent()` projection (the optional `subset` arg to `getStateDistrictGeometry`, assembled server-side into the route's `metros[]` payload, each with an `overviewBox`). **Leader-lines (HO 237):** each panel draws an amber source-rectangle on the overview (`overviewBoxForSubset`, in overview-projection coords) plus a two-line frustum from that rect to the inset's top corners (`components/MetroLeaderLines.tsx` ŌĆö an absolute pointer-events-none SVG overlay, recomputed via ResizeObserver, accounting for `xMidYMid meet` letterboxing); panels are ordered leftŌåÆright by `metroCenterX` so the frustum lines never cross. Both `RaceDistrictModal` and `PrimaryDistrictModal` render them; null-safe ŌĆö a state with no `METRO_PANELS` entry omits `metros[]` and shows overview-only. (Honest gap, documented in `metro-panels.ts`: CD06/Sacramento can only ride the Central Valley panel within the 2-cap, reaching ~15px rather than the ~22px floor ŌĆö not forced with a 3rd panel.) **Deferred (still):** the news block (no raceŌåÆnews linkage ŌĆö `news_mentions` is bill-keyed) and the `committee` meta field (degraded ŌĆö needs a `committee_members` join). The `DISPLAY_STALE_STATES` flag (HO 224, TX/CA/MO/OH/UT/NC) is still opt-in plumbing the modal does NOT yet act on ŌĆö it draws the 119th polygon everywhere (a TX-35 card reading "Lean R" on a D+34.8 incumbent is that known stale-boundary gap, not a bug).
- `/trends` ŌĆö corpus trend charts. Server page, **`export const dynamic = "force-dynamic"` (HO 243)** ŌĆö the corpus-wide Turso aggregations outgrew Next's ~60s static-export ceiling and the build began failing on the `/trends` prerender (pre-existing, surfaced by corpus growth), so it renders at request time; the query-layer `unstable_cache` still applies, so it's a small first-hit latency cost, not per-request load. Mounts, in order: **`BillsIntroTimeline` (HO 243** ŌĆö total introductions on a TRUE calendar axis: a hand-rolled SVG line of monthly introductions Jan-2025ŌåÆnow with year dividers and a dashed hollow-circle tail for the partial current month; backed by `getIntroductionsByMonth`, which shares `BillsTimeSeries`' universe ŌĆö current Congress, non-ceremonial, `topics IS NOT NULL` ŌĆö so the single line is the envelope of the stacked chart below it), then `BillsTimeSeries` (bills introduced per month, by topic; `getBillsByMonth`) and `TopicMixByChamber` (`getTopicMixByChamber`). SVG conventions are covered under "### Chart idiom".
- `/members/pass-rate` ŌĆö HO 89 legacy redirect to `/members?sort=passrate`; the standalone pass-rate view collapsed into the `/members` ranked list's VOLUME / PASS RATE toggle. Kept so old bookmarks resolve.
- `/search` ŌĆö global tabbed entity search (HO 129). URL: `?q=<query>&tab=<bills|members|news|reports>`. Receives `SearchBox` submissions from every page except `/bills` and `/members` (which keep their inline `?q=` filters). Page-level inline `SearchBox` lets the query stay editable. Counts for all four tabs run in parallel; only the active tab's result fetch runs. Active tab gets `aria-current="page"` + amber bottom border. Empty active tab with siblings shows `NO MATCHES IN <TAB> ┬Ę TRY <BEST> (N MATCHES) ŌåÆ` linked to the highest-count non-empty tab; all-tabs-empty shows the dead-end variant. Empty `?q=` shows the centered hint and zero counts (no 404). Bills tab reuses `BillRow compact` with pre-resolved watchlist membership; News tab reuses `NewsRow` with `linkBillToDetail`; Members shows name + party + state + chamber + bill count linked to `/members/[bioguide_id]`; Reports shows week + title + ~140-char snippet centered on the first match. All eight `search<Entity>` / `search<Entity>Count` helpers live in `lib/queries.ts`, `unstable_cache` with `revalidate: 600` and tag matching the entity (`bills`, `members`, `news-breaking`, `reports`). See `### Search` for full semantics.

Feed-shaped routes (`/bills`, `/stale`, `/changes`, `/watchlist`) share the same `HeaderBar` (count + last-updated MT) and render a `StageLegend` (party + stage legend) inline at the top of the list ŌĆö there is no footer legend component. The feed page passes `feedFilters` to `HeaderBar`, which swaps in a `<SearchBox />` (centered) and a filtered count display (`47 OF 1,643 BILLS ┬Ę "fentanyl"` with the numerator in `--accent-amber`).

### Search

Two surfaces (HO 129): inline page filters on `/bills` and `/members` (where the page natively renders the result list for `?q=`), and the global tabbed `/search?q=<query>&tab=<bills|members|news|reports>` route everywhere else.

- `components/SearchBox.tsx` is the only client search island. Reads `usePathname()` to decide where to route: paths starting with `/bills` or `/members` stay inline (preserves filter state via `searchParams.toString()`), everything else `router.push(/search?q=ŌĆ”)`. When already on `/search`, the active `tab` carries across keystrokes so a user mid-tab doesn't get bounced back to bills. 250ms debounce; `├Ś` clear button triggers the same effect via `setValue("")`. The `basePath` prop now only matters for the inline-stay destination.
- `/search` (HO 129) ŌĆö global tabbed search at `app/search/page.tsx`. Reads `?q` (sanitized via `sanitizeQ` ŌĆö trim + 200-char cap) and `?tab` (sanitized via `sanitizeSearchTab` against `SEARCH_TABS = ["bills","members","news","reports"]`; invalid falls back to `bills`). Runs all four `search<Entity>Count(q)` queries in parallel via `Promise.all`; only the active tab's `search<Entity>(q)` result fetch runs. Header shows `SEARCH ┬Ę <total> results`. Below header: inline `SearchBox`, count line (`145 RESULTS IN BILLS ┬Ę "education"`, numerator in `--accent-amber`), `SearchTabs` strip (active tab gets `aria-current="page"` and amber bottom border, zero-count tabs get `data-empty="true"` for 50% opacity), then the active tab's results. Empty active tab with non-empty siblings renders `NO MATCHES IN MEMBERS ┬Ę TRY BILLS (1,200 MATCHES) ŌåÆ` linked to the highest-count non-empty tab. Empty `?q=` shows the centered hint and zero counts. Backed by 8 cached helpers in `lib/queries.ts` (`searchBills`/`searchBillsCount`/`searchMembers`/ŌĆ”), each tagged with the matching invalidation tag (`bills`, `members`, `news-breaking`, `reports`).
- Bills search semantics (**HO 336 ŌĆö FTS5, was a LIKE**): `searchBills`/`searchBillsCount` `MATCH` the `bills_fts` FTS5 index (external content over `title/summary/sponsor_name`), join back to `bills` by rowid, gate on `summary IS NOT NULL` + non-ceremonial, and order by `bm25`. The match string is built by `buildBillsFtsMatch` (alphanumeric tokens, `len>=3` ŌåÆ prefix `tok*`, shorter ŌåÆ exact; AND across terms, OR across columns). **Global**: ignores stage/topic/cluster/chamber by design. **Behavior change from the LIKE:** `id` is no longer searchable in global /search (id tokens blew up the FTS ŌĆö see the Full-text search box above; id-substring search was already 500/non-functional under the LIKE); matching is token-prefix, not substring (so "tax" no longer matches inside "syntax"). The leading-`%` LIKE was the HO 335 `/search` 500. **`/bills?q=` (the inline feed filter) was wired to the same `bills_fts` in HO 338** ŌĆö see the Full-text search box above for its q-present/q-absent index split.
- Bill ID normalization: query and id are both lowercased and stripped of spaces/dashes before comparison, so `HR 2702`, `hr2702`, `hr-2702`, `2702`, and `119hr2702` all match `119-hr-2702`.
- Members search: `members.name OR members.state_name` LIKE-matched, `is_current=1` gate. Returns name + party + state + chamber + sponsored bill count. Reuses `bills_agg` CTE for the count. Rows link to `/members/[bioguide_id]`.
- News search: `news_mentions.article_title OR article_summary OR source`, INNER JOIN on bills with ceremonial gate. Reuses `NewsMention` shape so `SearchResultsNews` renders through the existing `NewsRow` (with `linkBillToDetail` so the bill rail jumps to `/bill/[id]` rather than `/bills`'s expand panel ŌĆö search intent is "find this thing").
- Reports search: `reports.title OR content_md`. `reports` table is ~5 rows ├Ś ~2KB markdown body, so the LIKE-scan is trivial. Result row includes a ~140-char snippet centered on the first match (markdown noise `#*_` collapsed to spaces).
- Inline `/bills?q=` (**HO 338 ŌĆö FTS5, was a LIKE**): when `q` is set, `getFeedBills` drives from `bills_fts` (`MATCH` + rowid join) and ANDs the rest via `buildFeedWhere(filters, {prefix:"bills.", skipQ:true})` ŌĆö composes with `?stage=`/`?topics=`/`?chamber=`/sort/pagination, date-sorted, count off the match, **no `INDEXED BY` hint** (it would block the FTS drive ŌĆö see the Full-text search box). When `q` is absent it's the HO 335 walk verbatim. `StageFilter`, `TopicFilter`, and `BillRow` thread `q` through their hrefs so search survives filter/expand changes. Empty results render a centered `NO BILLS MATCH "<q>"` block plus `[Clear search]` (preserves stage+topics). Match semantics match `/search`: token-prefix (not substring), spans title/summary/sponsor_name, id-substring dropped.
- Inline `/members?q=` semantics unchanged: name-only LIKE filter in `buildMemberWhere`.

### Ceremonial toggle (`?ceremonial=1`)

`components/CeremonialToggle.tsx` is a client island mounted in `HeaderBar`'s right cluster. It pushes `?ceremonial=1` on check, removes the param on uncheck, and preserves every other URL param including `expanded` (so flipping the filter doesn't collapse the open row). Label: `include ceremonial` unchecked, `including ceremonial` checked. Suppressed on `/watchlist` and `/bill/[id]` (HeaderBar gates on `feedFilters` being present).

URL plumbing mirrors `q` and `sponsor`: `StageFilter`, `TopicFilter`, `BillRow` accept a `ceremonial?: boolean` prop and append `ceremonial=1` to their generated hrefs. `SortDropdown`, `SearchBox`, the chamber `SegmentedToggle`, and `Pagination` all read or carry the existing URLSearchParams, so the toggle survives sort/search/chamber/pagination interactions automatically. Each list page (`/`, `/stale`, `/changes`, `/president`, `/members`) reads `params.ceremonial` via `sanitizeIncludeCeremonial`, threads it into `feedFilters`/`carry`, and passes it through to `BillRow`/`SponsorExpandedPanel`.

The standalone backfill is `npm run classify-ceremonial` ŌåÆ `scripts/classify-ceremonial.ts`. Concurrency 10, idempotent via `WHERE is_ceremonial IS NULL`, ~30 min for the full corpus, well under $1. After completion it POSTs to `REVALIDATE_URL` (with `Authorization: Bearer ${CRON_SECRET}`) to invalidate the `bills` tag ŌĆö a small `app/api/revalidate/route.ts` exists for that purpose. Without those env vars the script logs a hint instead of failing.

### Color palette (CSS vars on `:root` in `app/globals.css`)

```css
--bg-base: #0a0e14;            --bg-panel: #050709;
--bg-row-hover: #0f1620;       --border-strong: #1f2937;
--border-soft: #111820;
--text-primary: #e5e7eb;       --text-secondary: #cbd5e1;
--text-muted: #94a3b8;         --text-dim: #6b7280;
--accent-amber: #d97706;       --accent-amber-bright: #fbbf24;
--party-republican: #ef4444;   --party-democrat: #3b82f6;
--party-independent: #a78bfa;
--stage-introduced: #94a3b8;   --stage-committee: #06b6d4;
--stage-floor: #fbbf24;        --stage-other-chamber: #f59e0b;
--stage-president: #fb923c;    --stage-enacted: #10b981;
--vote-yea: #10b981;           --vote-nay: #f87171;
--vote-present: #fbbf24;       --vote-not-voting: #6b7280;
--kalshi: #4de4b2;             --poly: #2e5cff;
```

(Also on `:root`, documented in their own sections: `--market-up`/`--market-down`/`--ticker-closed` markets-tape direction + CLOSED wash; `--rail-house`/`--rail-senate` chamber rail.) **HO 287 source-tag tokens** `--kalshi #4de4b2` (turquoise) / `--poly #2e5cff` (blue) are scoped STRICTLY to the tier-3 source tags (`<SourceTag>`) ŌĆö never a general palette color. `--poly` sits near `--party-democrat` (#3b82f6), so by convention `P` is only ever rendered beside the turquoise `K` (the K/P pair), never alone in a party context where blue would read as "Democrat."

Vote tokens (handoff 79) are deliberately decoupled from party colors: `--vote-nay` is the softer `#f87171`, not `--party-republican`'s `#ef4444`, so a Democrat's nay vote doesn't read as a party-coded R chip. `--vote-yea` happens to share `#10b981` with `--stage-enacted` ŌĆö different semantics (a position vs. a stage), same green.

**Same-hue segmented bars need a structural separator (HO 207 rule).** Any horizontal bar whose segments share ONE base hue and encode rank by brightness/opacity (the primaries results bar's per-candidate share in one party tint; the same applies to the races DŌåöR spectrum and a future primaries-map coloring) MUST put a **1px hairline between adjacent segments** (the primaries bar uses `1px solid var(--bg-base)` with `box-sizing:border-box` so the border sits inside the `%` width). Brightness steps alone are NOT enough: at low opacity the steps wash out and two adjacent same-hue segments read as **one larger segment** ŌĆö e.g. a 46% leader + 25% runner-up in amber looked like a single ~70% bar labeled "46%". The hairline restores discrete-segment reading. (Pair it with `flex-shrink:0` + `min-width:0` on each segment so the rendered width tracks the value, not the label's min-content.)

### Stage indicators (arrow glyph + colored uppercase label)

`Ō¢Ė INTRO`, `Ō¢Ė COMMITTEE`, `Ō¢ĖŌ¢Ė FLOOR`, `Ō¢ĖŌ¢ĖŌ¢Ė OTHER CHAMBER`, `Ō¢ĖŌ¢ĖŌ¢ĖŌ¢Ė PRESIDENT`, `Ō£ō ENACTED`. Mobile abbreviates: `INTRO / COMM / FLR / OCHM / PRES / ENCT`. See `components/StageIndicator.tsx`.

### Topic colors + abbreviations (`lib/topic-colors.ts`)

23 enum values map to **7 color groups** + a catchall:

| Group | Color | Topics |
|---|---|---|
| Financial / commerce | `#a78bfa` purple | financial_services, taxes, budget, trade, consumer_protection |
| Tech | `#22d3ee` cyan | technology |
| Defense / foreign | `#34d399` teal | defense, foreign_policy, veterans |
| Environment / energy / agriculture | `#65a30d` green | environment, energy, agriculture |
| Social / labor | `#f472b6` pink | healthcare, education, labor, housing, social_security |
| Justice / civil | `#fb7185` red-pink | civil_rights, criminal_justice, immigration, elections |
| Infrastructure / ops | `#f59e0b` amber | transportation, government_operations |
| Catchall | `#6b7280` dim | other |

Display as 2-4-letter abbreviations (`FIN`, `HLTH`, `DEF`, `ENV`, `CRIM`, `GOV`, ŌĆ”) joined by ` ┬Ę ` between siblings. Multiple topics on the same bill share rendering: full list desktop, first + `+N` on mobile.

### Chip family (HO 287 ŌĆö canonical reference; `chip-family.html` was never committed)

The intended chip/tag vocabulary ŌĆö **three tiers, one size ladder 11 / 10 / 9px**:

- **Tier 1 ŌĆö bordered chips** (2px radius, weight 600). ID chip = solid `--accent-amber` border, 11px (the row anchor). Topic chip = the real topic hex (`topic-colors.ts`) at 45% alpha border, 10px.
- **Tier 2 ŌĆö stage pills** (bordered, 10px, format `LABEL ┬Ę age`). Inactive = `--text-dim` / `--border-strong`; current/active stage = its stage color at 50% alpha border.
- **Tier 3 ŌĆö text tags** (no border). Party = `--text-dim` (tint optional, off by default). **Source = brand-color letter, weight 600, 10px** (`K` = `--kalshi`, `P` = `--poly`) ŌĆö shared `<SourceTag>` (`components/SourceTag.tsx`). **Qualifier micro-tag = `--text-dim`, bordered, 9px** (EOD, MO) ŌĆö shared `<MicroTag>` (`components/MicroTag.tsx`).

**Only the tier-3 source + micro tags are on this system today (HO 287 additive half, retrofitted into the markets tape).** The **topic chip shipped (HO 316)** ŌĆö the shared bordered **`TopicChips`** (`components/TopicChips.tsx`): topic-color text + that color @45%-alpha border, the `CODE ┬Ę Full name` hover via the shared `Tooltip` primitive (underline-free `term` variant); imported by both the v2 feed row and `BillRow`, so every `BillRow` surface (`/bills` ┬Ę `/stale` ┬Ę `/changes` ┬Ę `/president` ┬Ę `/watchlist`) gets it. The lone borderless **`TopicTags`** holdout is **`/bill/[id]`** (backlog). The remaining **id/stage/party** chips are NOT yet migrated and diverge from the spec: `BillIdRail` is a vertical chamber-colored block (not a chip), `.stage-pill` is 11px with a full-color (not 50%-alpha) border, `.v2f-id` is the closest (bordered amber 11px). That migration is its own **B6 arc** (backlog QUEUED) ŌĆö work from this spec, not from the absent `chip-family.html`.

### Typography

- `var(--font-mono)` (`ui-monospace, JetBrains Mono, ŌĆ”`) on `body` ŌĆö the app default. **Sans carve-out (HO 296ŌĆō300, extended HO 317):** the all-mono rule now has ONE exception ŌĆö bill **titles** (the v2 feed row + `/bills` `BillRow`), the expanded panel's **summary**, and the sponsor card's natural name render in the **`--sans`** token (`system-ui, -apple-system, "Segoe UI", Roboto, sans-serif`, defined in `:root`). It's the only non-mono face; everything else (chrome, labels, ids, metrics, meta) stays monospace. The carve-out is for prose readability on the feed.
- Size tiers (post handoff 20 readability bump; previous values shown in parentheses):
  - **12px** (was 10px) ŌĆö column headers, badges, topic tags, footer legend, dropdown labels, button text, filter chip labels.
  - **13px** (was 11px) ŌĆö dates, search input, brand mark, dim secondary text, count line auxiliaries.
  - **14px** (was 12px) ŌĆö body content: bill IDs in rows, sponsor names, stage indicators, expanded summaries (`text-sm leading-relaxed`). **The feed-row bill TITLE is larger ŌĆö `.feed-row .row-title` is 18px as of HO 187** (16ŌåÆ18; shared with the dashboard ACTIVITY feed, which grew too).
  - **15px** (was 13px) ŌĆö bill detail page subtitle (`<h1>` text under the bill ID).
  - **16px** (was 14px) ŌĆö bill detail page bill ID, the most prominent number on the page.
- Letter-spacing `0.5px` on uppercase labels. Sentence case for prose.
- When you bump a tier, also bump the `.feed-row`/`.sponsor-row` fixed column widths in `globals.css` to keep stage labels and dates from overflowing ŌĆö the current widths are sized for the tiers above. Don't reuse the old values.
- **Header type scale (HO 281, desktop only).** The masthead/header breadcrumb title is **26px** and the nav is **16px** on desktop, with the active nav item carrying a **2px `--accent-amber` underline** ŌĆö all scoped `@media (min-width: 701px)`, so the **mobile (HO 244) sizes are untouched** (the brand stays 20px below 701px). The bump raised the header's one-line threshold to ~1420px, so a 1366px laptop reflows the counts + nav to a clean 2nd line (oddities). The masthead + header render on BOTH `/` (`HomeHeader`) and `/dashboard-v2` (`DashboardV2Header`), so a change to either lands on both.

### Layout grid

Layout is **full-width fluid** ŌĆö no `max-w-*` cap on the outer container. Pages, `HeaderBar`, and `StageLegend` all stretch to the viewport with `w-full` and a small `px-4` gutter. The `1fr` title column inside `BillRow` and `SponsorRow` absorbs the extra width on wide displays. If a future page feels too sparse at 2400px+, the right fix is to add `max-w-[1200px]` to the offending column (e.g. the bill summary paragraph), not to re-cap the outer container.

**Spacing tokens (HO 131).** Five CSS custom properties in `:root` drive block-level rhythm; defined once in `globals.css`. Use these instead of ad-hoc px values for block gaps, padding, and margins.

- `--space-xs: 4px` ŌĆö tightest separation; chip gaps, dot offsets
- `--space-sm: 8px` ŌĆö small block padding (e.g. compact label margins, narrow row gaps)
- `--space-md: 12px` ŌĆö default block gap (grid gap, pane padding, header internal spacing)
- `--space-lg: 16px` ŌĆö generous block padding (lead prose padding, main horizontal gutter on home)
- `--space-xl: 24px` ŌĆö outer page gutter / large section breaks (home main padding)

Inner-row paddings (`.feed-row`, `.topic-dist-row`, `.funnel-row`, `.top-stalls-row`, etc.) keep their custom hardcoded px values ŌĆö those drive per-row visual density, not block rhythm. The token scale is intentionally scoped to layout/structure.

`--home-header-height: 200px` is **dead code**. It once fed `.home-grid`'s no-scroll `calc(100vh - var(--home-header-height) - ŌĆ”)` math, but that calc was removed when the dashboard became scrollable (the HO 150 reflow ŌĆö see the `/` entry, which already flags this var as dead); the only surviving reference is a comment in `globals.css`. History: HO 133 bumped it 180pxŌåÆ240px when Stage Distribution + Color Key moved from grid quadrants into the header band; it now sits at 200px, unused. Safe to delete ŌĆö left in `:root` as a harmless no-op.

`.feed-row` grid is post-HO-125 redesigned, with HO 148 swapping the navigation Link for an expand-on-click div role=button on full rows:

- Default: `1fr 40px 36px` ŌĆö interactive row ┬Ę media-attention cell (HO 130) ┬Ę watch star
- `has-days-since` (used by `/stale` and by `/bills?stage=president` when no explicit `?sort` ŌĆö the HO 151 president alias path): `1fr 90px 40px 36px` ŌĆö adds days-since column
- Compact (used by `ActivityTicker`, `SearchResultsBills`, `/patterns` drilldown, `/committee/[systemCode]` recent activity): `1fr 40px 28px` ŌĆö slimmer rail, smaller star, still link-only (no expand)
- Below 700px: media-attention and days-since are hidden via `display: none`; the row collapses to `1fr 32px` (or `1fr 28px` compact). Filter chips wrap; date column hidden via `.col-date`; stage label switches to short form (`.show-mobile` / `.show-desktop`); topics show first + `+N`.

The interactive row wrapper is itself a two-column grid (`56px 1fr`) holding `BillIdRail` and `row-content` (title + StagePillStrip + row-meta). HO 148 removed the inline summary excerpt (`.row-summary`) and the `View detail ŌåÆ` text (`.row-view-detail`) from the row meta ŌĆö both moved into the expanded panel. The media-attention chip (HO 130) and watch star sit *outside* the interactive wrapper as separate grid cells so their own anchors/buttons don't nest inside it.

### Mobile header + nav drawer (spec 15a)

**The header is two components, not one.** Any mobile/header work must keep this split straight (it tripped up the original 15a spec, which assumed a single header with a secondary nav row that HO 134 had already deleted):

- **`HomeHeader`** ŌĆö dashboard (`/`) only. Holds the unified breadcrumb path (`BreadcrumbMasthead` ŌåÆ `Congressional Terminal:\119TH\Dashboard>`, HO 185 ŌĆö was the `Congressional Terminal:\>` `TerminalPrompt`; **HO 244 dropped it 36pxŌåÆ20px** so the stat readout fits beside it), the **HO 244 STAT READOUT** to its right (`n bills tracked ┬Ę n in committee ┬Ę n on the floor ┬Ę n other chamber ┬Ę n enacted` ŌĆö replaced HO 178's lead-in prose), the blinking **desktop-only** cursor at the **readout end** (`.home-readout-caret`, HO 244 ŌĆö was the lead-prose end per HO 230; one of three motion exceptions), the `┬Ę LAST SYNC ŌĆ”` subhead (the time cycles zones, HO 183; **`N BILLS TRACKED` moved up into the readout**), the shared single `<MarketsTape />` (HO 234 collapse; was `DualMarketsTape`), and its own `.home-header-nav`.
- **`HeaderBar`** ŌĆö every other page. **HO 323 standardized the inner-page chrome; HO 325 added the sync subhead.** The live stack is **title row (breadcrumb path + path-end caret) ŌåÆ `┬Ę LAST SYNC <time>` subhead ŌåÆ nav row ŌåÆ page content** (the page's own control strip / topics band / legend+pagination render below). The **title bar is the breadcrumb path ONLY** ŌĆö `BreadcrumbMasthead` renders `Congressional Terminal:\119TH\<Section>[\<Detail>]>_` via `breadcrumbSegments(basePath, ŌĆ”)` at **20px** (sized above the nav so the title dominates), with the blinking `_` glued to the path end. **HO 185** introduced the breadcrumb path (replacing the `CBT // 119th Congress` title; the dead `variant="dashboard"` branch was deleted). The **`┬Ę LAST SYNC <time>` subhead** (`.header-sync-sub`, **HO 325**) sits on its own line between the title and the nav, matching the dashboard `HomeHeader` subhead exactly ŌĆö same label, the HO 183 zone-cycling `CyclingTimestamp`, reading the same global source `getCorpusStats(true).lastSync` (filter-independent, so a filtered inner page can't drift from the dashboard's instant). It is the **third cycling timestamp** (see Date formatting). The **nav is on its own full-width row** below the subhead ŌĆö `.header-nav-row` wrapping `PrimaryNav variant="home"` (the dashboard's `.home-header-nav` bracketed-active styling), no longer inline beside the path. **The markets tape and the inline title-bar count/sync metadata (`┬Ę N BILLS ┬Ę UPDATED MT`) were REMOVED from inner pages (HO 323)** ŌĆö tickers + the stat readout are dashboard-only now; this superseded the HO 202/234 model (a single `<MarketsTape />` mounted in `HeaderBar`, tape on every page) and the HO 189 inline sync strip (`ŌĆ”>_ ┬Ę N BILLS ┬Ę UPDATED MT`, filter-aware, static `formatLastUpdated`). The **HO 195 Members-only `cursorAtEnd`/`liftSyncContrast` divergence** is gone with the inline sync it anchored ŌĆö the caret falls back to the path end on every page (`BreadcrumbMasthead`'s `cursor` prop, default `true`, keeps it glued to the `>` everywhere). **HO 326 swept the dead code** the 323 transition left behind: the count/`getFeedStats`/`clusterName` computations, the call-site count props (`countMode`/`staleCounts`/ŌĆ”/`pageCount`/`pageTitle`/`cursorAtEnd`/`liftSyncContrast`), the orphaned `.header-titlebar-sync` / `.header-titlebar-nav` classes, and the now-unused `MarketsTape`/`getClusterPattern`/`formatLastUpdated`/`FeedCount` imports. **HO 187** had earlier consolidated the inner chrome into bands and moved `SearchBox` + `CeremonialToggle` out to the page's own control strip; `/bills` ┬Ę `/changes` ┬Ę `/stale` pass `pageOwnsControls` so `HeaderBar` suppresses its transitional legacy search+ceremonial band and each renders its own control strip, and **HO 195 migrated `/members` onto `pageOwnsControls` too** ŌĆö so every page is on the pattern and the legacy band no longer renders for any page (the band + prop stay in `HeaderBar` only as the now-unexercised fallback). `/members` keeps `feedFilters` (it still gates the suppressed search/ceremonial controls) but drops the redundant `search billsŌĆ”` input and relocates INCLUDE CEREMONIAL into its own filter row.
- **`GroupTabs`** (sub-nav strip, HO 134) is separate chrome below the header. The per-page **`page-masthead`** heroes (`Feed:\>` / `Members:\>`, HO 154.4) were **removed in HO 185** ŌĆö the section name now lives once, in the breadcrumb path. `TerminalPrompt`, `.page-masthead`, and `.home-cursor-title` are now unused no-ops left in place for a later sweep.

Nav is **one flat row of 7 group landings** (`NAV_ITEMS` in `HeaderBar.tsx`: Dashboard ┬Ę Bills ┬Ę Members ┬Ę Electoral ┬Ę Patterns ┬Ę Reports ┬Ę Watchlist). **HO 230 restyled it to a text-only path style** (`PrimaryNav`): icons dropped (the `icon` field lingers on `NAV_ITEMS` but isn't rendered), each item `\`-prefixed, the active item wrapped in amber `[ \LABEL ]` brackets (bracket space reserved on every item so the row doesn't shift) + amber-bright label + amber-bright underline, and the items split into **3 groups by divider**. **The `Bills|News` label is gone** ŌĆö the item is now just `Bills` (the `feed` group key is unchanged internally). The old secondary STALE┬ĘCHANGES┬ĘPRESIDENT┬ĘWATCHLIST row was removed by HO 134; those destinations live inside `GroupTabs` on the landing pages.

**Mobile nav = the inline nav, wrapping (HO 156 + HO 161).** There is no hamburger; the inline nav *is* the mobile nav at every width, and **both** header navs wrap to a second row when cramped: the **dashboard** nav `.home-header-nav` has `flex-wrap: wrap` (`globals.css`), and the **HeaderBar** nav `.header-nav` is `flex flex-wrap items-center` (`HeaderBar.tsx`, added in HO 161) ŌĆö **HO 185 moved it onto its own full-width row** (`.header-nav-row`), then **HO 187 moved it back into the title bar** beside the path (the `.header-nav-row` is gone; the path is sized larger than the nav so the title still dominates, and the nav wraps under only for the deepest paths). Before HO 161, `.header-nav` was `flex items-center` with no wrap and no overflow handling, so it clipped on a narrow phone ŌĆö HO 160 flagged this (one draft of that sweep mis-stated it as already having `overflow-x-auto`; it never did). Both navs use static wrap ŌĆö no scroll-x / motion exception.

**`MobileNavDrawer` is built but DORMANT.** `components/MobileNavDrawer.tsx` ŌĆö one `"use client"` island, mounted in both headers, fed the same `NAV_ITEMS` ŌĆö stays in the tree, but `.mobile-nav` is `display: none` at **all** widths, so the hamburger never renders. It was the original HO 156 plan; the wrapping inline nav made it unnecessary at this nav count. Kept for revival if the nav ever grows past what wraps cleanly ŌĆö the exact `@media (max-width: 700px)` block to re-add lives in the `.mobile-nav` comment in `globals.css`, including the cascade-order caveat that bit the first attempt (an equal-specificity base `.home-header-nav { display: flex }` sits *later* in the file and wins over an earlier media-query hide). When revived: instant `display` toggle (no slide ŌĆö stays inside the static-below-1024 constraint, not a motion exception), dismiss on nav-tap + hamburger re-tap, with tap-outside-to-dismiss and an in-drawer close glyph deferred to **15c**'s global touch convention (which must layer onto, not conflict with, this model).

**Font-size bands + header collapse (HO 157).** Sizing principle: **one hero per surface grows on mobile; everything else holds or moves to the drawer ŌĆö nothing shrinks.** (The original 15a spec shrank the title on mobile, which inverted the real shipped behavior; this is the correction. Small screens need the primary mark bigger, not smaller.) All Ōēź1024 values below are the real shipped values, so desktop stays **pixel-unchanged**.

| Element | Ōēź1024 | 700ŌĆō1023 | <700 | Behavior |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| HomeHeader prompt (`.home-header-prompt-row .terminal-prompt`) | **20px** (HO 244) | 20px | 20px | **HO 244 flattened it to a flat 20px at all widths** (word-spacing ŌłÆ6px), down from the 36/18/24 HO 162 hero ŌĆö the stat readout now shares line 1, so the brand stops being the grow-hero |
| HomeHeader stat readout + caret (`.home-stat-readout` / `.home-readout-caret`) | 14px | 14px | 14px | **HO 244 replaced the HO 178 lead-in prose** with the stat readout (`n bills tracked ┬Ę ŌĆ”`); holds 14px and wraps below the brand on narrow widths via the prompt row's flex-wrap. The blinking caret rides the readout end and is **desktop-only** (hidden `<700`, where a trailing caret would float mid-stack). |
| HomeHeader subhead (`.home-header-meta`) | 11px | 11px | 11px | Holds; abbreviates to `┬Ę h:MM AM/PM MT ┬Ę N BILLS` <700 by dropping LAST SYNC / TRACKED via `.show-desktop` |
| HeaderBar breadcrumb path (`ŌĆ”>_`, HO 185/187) | **20px** | 20px | 20px | The path is the title, sized above the nav (HO 187). HO 323 put the nav on its own row, so the path no longer shares its line with the (removed) inline sync or the nav; a deep detail path wraps within the title row. |
| HeaderBar LAST SYNC subhead (`.header-sync-sub`, HO 325) | 11px | 11px | 11px | The `┬Ę LAST SYNC <time>` cycling subhead on its own line between the path and the nav row (mirrors the dashboard `.home-header-meta`). |
| HeaderNav / home-nav | **14px** | 14px | 14px | Both navs are now the SAME `.home-header-nav` styling ŌĆö the dashboard mounts `PrimaryNav variant="home"` and inner pages mount it via `HeaderBar` (HO 323), so the old 13px `.header-nav` (`variant="bar"`) is retired/unused. Both **wrap** when cramped (`flex-wrap`, HO 161); static, no scroll-x. Drawer dormant ŌĆö see above. *(Mobile base values; HO 281 lifts titleŌåÆ26 / navŌåÆ16 at Ōēź701px ŌĆö not yet reflected per-column here.)* |
| `page-masthead` (`Feed:\>` etc.) | ŌĆö | ŌĆö | ŌĆö | **Removed in HO 185** ŌĆö the section name now lives in the breadcrumb path |
| `GroupTabs` (`.search-tabs`) | 14px | 14px | 14px | Holds; **wraps** when cramped (`flex-wrap`, HO 161 ŌĆö replaced the <700 `overflow-x:auto` scroll) |

- **Breadcrumb sizing scope (HO 185 ŌĆö was the page-masthead anti-grow rule).** The per-page `page-masthead` hero was removed, so its anti-grow rule is moot, but the same CSS scoping now governs the breadcrumb path: the 36px (Ōēź1024) / 24px (`<700`) grow is scoped to `.home-header-prompt-row .terminal-prompt`, so the **dashboard** path is the hero while the **HeaderBar** path (bare `.terminal-prompt`, no `.home-header-prompt-row` ancestor) holds at **20px** (HO 187, sized larger than the 13px nav) on every other page.
- **Overflow pass ŌĆö resolved (HO 161).** The #6/#7 overflow cluster is closed with one convention: **static wrap, no scroll-x.** GroupTabs `.search-tabs` added `flex-wrap` and its <700 `overflow-x:auto` was replaced with `flex-wrap: wrap`; `.header-nav` added `flex flex-wrap`; `.filter-chips` already wrapped (`flex flex-wrap` + a <700 `flex-wrap: wrap` rule); the markets tape stays `display:none` <700 (HO 156). Scroll-x with an edge fade was rejected ŌĆö it's a sub-1024 motion exception, and wrap is the no-motion default.
- **Markets tape hidden <700px (HO 156 follow-up).** `.markets-tape` is `display: none` below 700px (CSS-only, both mount points ŌĆö dashboard `HomeHeader` and the global `HeaderBar`). It's a dense desktop strip that wraps poorly on phones and reads stale on the daily refresh; not worth the vertical space above breaking-news / stage-distribution. The HO 142 data layer stays mounted (ticks still fetched), so this is purely visual. The desktop tape and its marquee-on-touch question (owned by the #6 overflow pass) are untouched.
- **Deferred `<700` thread (HO 194ŌĆō200, open).** The HO 198/200 3-column member card (`.sponsor-card-grid`) ships a *minimal* `<700` stack guard (single column, border-rightŌåÆborder-bottom) but no real mobile pass; the HO 194 120├Ś144 sponsor hover card and the HO 195 Members chrome (cursor/contrast/filter-row) are desktop-tuned and not mobile-specced. All three are open `<700` follow-ups ŌĆö note, not yet specced.

### Click-to-expand accordion (HO 148)

Full rows (non-compact) are click-to-expand accordions. **This reverses HO 125's inline-summary-as-primary decision** ŌĆö the inline summary excerpt is gone, the collapsed row is just title + meta line + chevron, the full summary lives in the expanded panel. The reversal is deliberate (design language matured into spec 4 expand-as-primary).

- `components/BillRowList.tsx` (client) wraps every full-row consumer. Owns the single-open `expandedId` state and a per-bill `Map<billId, PanelData>` cache so re-expanding a row never refetches. Consumers: `/bills` (incl. the `?stage=president` alias), `/watchlist`, `/changes`, `/stale`, `/members/[bioguideId]` Sponsored block.
- `components/BillRow.tsx` is now a `"use client"` component. When `onToggle` is provided (full rows via `BillRowList`), the outer `<Link>` is replaced with `<div role="button" tabIndex={0} aria-expanded>` that toggles on click and on Enter/Space. The expanded panel renders below the row inside the same `<li>` via `grid-column: 1 / -1`. When `onToggle` is omitted (compact path or any direct caller), the original HO 125 `<Link>` navigation is preserved ŌĆö compact rows on `ActivityTicker`/`SearchResultsBills`/`/patterns`/`/committee/[systemCode]` stay link-only. **HO 192:** the collapsed row's short sponsor name (e.g. `HARRIS`) gets the same highlight + hover card as the expanded panel, **gated on `expandable && sponsor_bioguide_id`** ŌĆö link-only/compact rows wrap the whole row in a real `<Link>`, where a nested member `<a>` would be invalid HTML, so they keep plain text (and don't SELECT the bioguide/photo anyway). `/bills`-only.
- `components/SponsorHoverName.tsx` (client, HO 192; refined HO 194) ŌĆö the shared sponsor affordance used by both the expanded panel's SPONSOR row and the collapsed `BillRow`. Renders the member-link `<a>` (with `stopPropagation` so it navigates without toggling) plus a **pure-CSS hover/focus card** (matches the tape/topic-chip popover idiom): a **120├Ś144 photo** (5:6 bioguide ratio ŌĆö HO 194 enlarged it from 46├Ś60) from `sponsor_depiction_url` (`onError` ŌåÆ party-colored initials, the `SponsorPhoto`/`MemberHeader` pattern), photo-left/text-right with the text top-aligned, on a **320px** card. **Three text lines in natural order** (HO 194, NOT the row's "Last, First"): `Rep./Sen. First Last` (prefix from `bill_type`; built from the threaded `sponsor_first_name`/`sponsor_last_name` so it's parse-safe ŌĆö "King, Angus S., Jr." ŌåÆ "Angus King") / party-district bracket `[R-MD-1]` (party-colored; at-large ŌåÆ `-At Large`, Senate ŌåÆ no district segment) / `State ┬Ę Nth District` (full state via `lib/states`, ordinal via `lib/format`; Senate ŌåÆ `┬Ę Senate`, at-large ŌåÆ `┬Ę At-Large District`). A `label` prop sets the trigger text (panel = full `sponsor_name`, row = short last name); the card content is always derived from the bill/member fields, so it reads the same either way. **At-rest affordance (HO 194):** the trigger name shows a **solid amber underline at rest** (`.sponsor-hover > a`, scoped so other `bill-expanded-link` uses are untouched) so the interaction is discoverable; hover intensifies to `--accent-amber-bright`. The card is **absolute + opaque (`--bg-row-hover`) + border + shadow** so it overlays without shifting layout ŌĆö **CSS popover, not a portal**: there is no `overflow:hidden` on any ancestor of `.row-meta` (only `.row-title` and the leaf `truncate` spans clip, neither an ancestor of the card), so the absolute card escapes cleanly. (The per-row topic-code portal was a property of the HO 147 Tooltip primitive, not a row clip.) Party normalization is inlined (not imported from `lib/queries`, which would pull `next/cache` into the client bundle).
- **HO 317 ŌĆö the FULL `/bills` expand is now the shared `BillExpandPanel`** (the SAME rich panel the dashboard `/` renders ŌĆö see the B6 section below ŌĆö differing only in trigger: `/bills` click vs dashboard hover). `BillRowList` renders it for full rows and owns the lazy fetch. **`BillExpandedPanel` is now the COMPACT path only** (the dashboard-classic ACTIVITY ticker, `compact` variant). The `STAGE PIPELINE ŌåÆ two columns` layout described in the next three bullets is the **superseded** pre-317 full layout (kept for history); the live full panel is `BillExpandPanel` with the shared `BillStageBar`.
- `components/BillExpandedPanel.tsx` (client). **HO 191 redesigned it** from a vertical stack (summary ŌåÆ meta list ŌåÆ timeline strip ŌåÆ news ŌåÆ buttons) into: **full-width STAGE PIPELINE ŌåÆ two columns** (the collapsed row above is the header). Everything below renders instantly from the already-loaded `FeedBill`; only committees + news lazy-load.
  - **STAGE PIPELINE** (replaces the old HO 188 timeline strip entirely). Six nodes INTRO ┬Ę COMMITTEE ┬Ę FLOOR ┬Ę OTHER CHAMBER ┬Ę PRESIDENT ┬Ę ENACTED in `--stage-*` colors. Reached = filled dot; **current** = larger bright marker (panel-bg ring + node-color halo) + bold label; unreached = dim hollow dot. Connector colored up to current, `--border-strong` after (pseudo-element half-segments meeting at each dot center; dot centers pinned to y=8 so they align across the size change). Dates appear under a node only when stored: **INTRO from `introduced_date`, the current stage from `stage_changed_at`** (present on ~4% of bills ŌĆö HO 188); intermediate reached stages show label only (no per-stage history is stored). **Dead/failed bills:** no schema signal for death, so the last-reached stage just renders as **current** (claims position, not death ŌĆö no struck/dimmed state); enacted fills the whole pipeline. **Suppressed entirely** when `stage` is NULL (123 unsummarized) or off-path `other` (`ALLOWED_STAGES.indexOf` ŌåÆ ŌłÆ1) ŌĆö an all-unreached strip would falsely read as "reached nothing."
  - **TWO COLUMNS.** LEFT (~1.6fr, `border-right`): SUMMARY (`--text-secondary`) then RELATED NEWS (Ōēż5 matched mentions, `[SOURCE]` + headline link; **HO 191 added an explicit "No related news" empty state** ŌĆö `--text-dim`, reusing `.bill-expanded-news-empty` ŌĆö instead of hiding the section). RIGHT (~1fr, darker `--bg-panel`): the HO 188 enrichment label-rows ŌĆö **SPONSOR** (links to `/members/[bioguideId]` when `sponsor_bioguide_id` is present, plain text otherwise; **HO 192 hover card** ŌĆö see below), **COSPONSORS** count (`cosponsor_count`; the *list* isn't stored, so count-only), **COMMITTEE** (deduped newest-activity-per-systemCode, each linking to `/committee/[systemCode]`), **INTRODUCED**, **LAST ACTION** (stacked label-above-value since it's long) ŌĆö **the STAGE label row was removed** (the pipeline owns position) ŌĆö then two action chips: `full bill page ŌåÆ` (real `<a href={/bill/[id]}>` so cmd/middle-click new-tab works) and `congress.gov ŌåŚ` (soft-border variant).
  - **HO 192 sponsor hover card.** The linked SPONSOR name carries an additive hover/focus card (shared `SponsorHoverName`, below) ŌĆö photo + full name + party-state ŌĆö and the `<a>` still navigates. `/bills`-only (rides `sponsor_depiction_url`). Unmatched sponsors (no bioguide) stay plain text.
  - **`compact` variant** (dashboard ACTIVITY expand, HO 164): **pipeline + summary only** ŌĆö drops the right metadata column AND related news, and **skips the `GET /api/bill/[id]/panel` fetch entirely ŌåÆ 0 queries** (full `/bills` stays at 2: committees + news on first open, reported up to BillRowList for caching). A deliberate content reduction on the glance surface (it previously showed committees + news via the shared full panel). The compact pipeline abbreviates **OTHER CHAMBER ŌåÆ "OTHER CH."** (an optional `compactLabel` on the stage table) so all six nodes stay single-line at the smaller width; the full `/bills` pipeline keeps "OTHER CHAMBER".
  - Similar/related bills stay **dropped** (only regex `cluster_id`, not real topical similarity); full action-history timeline stays **deferred** (not stored). The `lib/queries` import is **type-only** (the runtime `normalizePartyVariant` would pull `next/cache` into the client bundle ŌĆö party normalization is inlined in `SponsorHoverName`); the color map is a typed `as const` (for `noUncheckedIndexedAccess`).
- `app/api/bill/[id]/panel/route.ts` is the lazy-load endpoint. GET ŌåÆ `{ committees, news }` from the existing cached helpers (`getBillCommittees` tag `committees`, `getNewsForBill` tag `news-breaking`). Single-open caps in-flight to one extra fetch at any moment ŌĆö far cheaper than the alternative of pre-rendering 50 hidden panels at page load.
- Chevron `Ō¢Ė` lives at the end of the row meta line. Rotates 90┬░ instantly (no transition) and switches to `--accent-amber` when open. Open row also gets `--bg-row-hover` background.
- `MediaAttentionCell` and `WatchStar` both call `e.stopPropagation()` on click so the press chip and star don't toggle the row when clicked. Action chips and committee/news links inside the panel also stopPropagation so they navigate cleanly.
- Cosponsor party split deliberately not surfaced ŌĆö `bills.cosponsor_count` is the only cosponsor data the sync stores today (HO 148 Phase 1 finding). Cosponsor-list ingestion is a future handoff.
- URL state (`?open=<billId>`) deliberately deferred. Expand is pure client state; zero server traffic per toggle. If deep-linking demand shows up later, the param slots in alongside `?topics= ?stage= ?q= ?sponsor= ?sort= ?page= ?chamber= ?ceremonial= ?cluster=` without collisions.

**Expand-state, two idioms by rendering model (HO 155).** The single-open accordion is carried two ways, on purpose:

- **Client surfaces** (`/bills`, `/stale`, `/watchlist`, `/changes`, member-detail Sponsored block) all render through `BillRowList`, which holds open state in `useState` and lazy-fetches panel data client-side via `/api/bill/[id]/panel`. It is already one shared component ŌĆö no duplication to unify.
- **Members list** (`app/members/page.tsx`) is a server component. Open state is `?expanded=<bioguideId>` read from `searchParams`; the open panel's data (stats/topics/recent bills/committees/affiliations) is fetched server-side and rendered into the initial HTML. Navigation is `<Link replace scroll={false}>`, so row toggles don't pile up history.

This is **not** drift to be unified behind a shared hook. Members is URL-driven precisely because a deep-linked open member panel is shareable content that must server-render into HTML ŌĆö a client `useExpandState`-style hook would paint the row closed, then hydrate and fetch, degrading exactly that property. The feed is client-driven because nobody deep-links an open feed row and URL-syncing it just litters history. Different jobs, correctly different idioms ŌĆö the split is by *rendering model* (server-component URL state vs client-component `useState`), not by a swappable backing store. HO 155 evaluated extracting a `useExpandState({ persist })` hook and rejected it: the client surface is already one component, and the members server-render can't call a client hook without a rewrite (+ a new `/api/member/[id]/panel`) that would undo its deep-link benefit.

### Markets tape (HO 149)

Markets ticker tape ŌĆö **dashboard-only** (HO 323 removed it from inner pages; `HeaderBar` no longer mounts it). It renders on two surfaces: the live dashboard `/` (`DashboardV2Header`) shows the **B2 two-tape stack** ŌĆö a scrolling **MARKETS** strip over a scrolling **ODDS** strip (detail below) ŌĆö and the preserved legacy `/dashboard-classic` (`HomeHeader`) shows a **single bare static** `<MarketsTape />`. One shared component, `MarketsTape` (server) ŌåÆ `MarketsTapeClient`; its `symbols`/`pairs`/`kind`/`scroll`/`reverse`/`label` props drive both shapes (bare = no props ŌåÆ the default set, static; B2 = the two configured strips). *(Lineage, compressed: HO 178 dual counter-scroll ŌåÆ HO 185/202 `DualMarketsTape` app-wide ŌåÆ HO 234 one line app-wide ŌåÆ HO 323 dashboard-only + HO 289/290 two-tape B2; `DualMarketsTape` is deleted.)* Feeds off `getLatestMarketTicks()` (HO 142). **The roster lives in `lib/markets.ts` (`MARKET_SYMBOLS`)** ŌĆö FMP intraday indices/equities (SPX/NDQ + the HO 289 NVDA/AAPL/MSFT/GOOGL/LMT), FRED EOD (`TNX`/`WTI`) + monthly (`CPI`/`UNEMP`, `cadence:"monthly"`), and Kalshi+Polymarket prediction **pairs** (`SHUTDOWN`, `FEDCUT` Jul + `FEDCUT-SEP`, `RECESSION`, each with a `POLY-*` half). `MarketSymbol` carries `cadence`/`source`/`units`/`kalshiKind`/`polyKind` and **(HO 302)** `kalshiEvent` + `polyMonth` to pin a specific Kalshi event / Polymarket month ŌĆö the mechanism behind July vs September as distinct fed-cut symbols (`FEDCUT-SEP` = `KXFEDDECISION-26SEP` / `polyMonth:"september"`). Newly-added symbols show `ŌĆö` until a prior-session reference exists.

  **The two shapes in detail (both dashboard-only since HO 323; surfaces remapped by the HO 311 swap):**
  - **Bare `<MarketsTape />` on `/dashboard-classic` (HomeHeader, the preserved legacy dashboard) ONLY** ŌĆö **STATIC** full-width row (HO 251 dropped the crawl; the 8-symbol trim is what made it fit). It EXCLUDES the **v2-only** symbols (HO 287/289 `BARE_TAPE_EXCLUDED` in `MarketsTape` = `source="polymarket"` Ōł¬ `bareTape:false`), so it stays the **8-symbol** static set (SPX/NDQ/TNX/CPI/UNEMP/SHUTDOWN/FEDCUT/WTI). The HO 289 equities + HO 290 RECESSION carry `bareTape:false` and the Polymarket halves are source-excluded, so they ride the v2 scrolling tapes ONLY and the static bare row never grows past 8 (it can't fit more).
  - **The dashboard `/` (`DashboardV2Header`; was `/dashboard-v2` before the HO 311 swap)** ŌĆö a **TWO-tape stack** the **B2 arc (HO 289ŌĆō294)** expanded: a **MARKETS** strip over an **ODDS** strip (HO 290 relabelled SIGNALSŌåÆODDS), **both `scroll` + COUNTER-SCROLLING (HO 291: MARKETS RŌåÆL, ODDS LŌåÆR via `animation-direction: reverse` on `.markets-tape-track--reverse`, threaded by a `reverse` prop)**, with **widened opaque-edge fades (HO 291: `label::after`/`meta::before` 72px on the scroll tapes vs 28px on the bare static row)** so ticks dissolve at the bounds instead of hard-cutting. **MARKETS roster** = `["SPX","NDQ","NVDA","AAPL","MSFT","GOOGL","LMT","TNX","WTI","CPI","UNEMP"]` ŌĆö indices + the **five HO 289 equities** (NVDA/AAPL/MSFT/GOOGL/LMT, intraday FMP `/stable/quote`, **no freshness badge**; RTX/NOC/GD were specced but 402 on FMP free tier, HO 288) + 10Y/WTI (EOD) + **CPI/UNEMP (HO 290 relocated here from the second strip, MO badge)**. **ODDS roster** (prediction-markets-ONLY, all **dual-source K/P**): `SHUTDOWN` ┬Ę **`FEDCUT` (FED CUT JUL) ┬Ę `FEDCUT-SEP` (FED CUT SEP ŌĆö HO 302, the September Fed decision pinned via `kalshiEvent`/`polyMonth`; same `label:"FED CUT"` disambiguated by `showMonth` appending the resolution month from each primary's `marketDate`)** ┬Ę **`RECESSION` (HO 290 ŌĆö Kalshi `KXRECSSNBER` single-yes + Polymarket `us-recession-by-end-of-2026`)**, each paired with its `POLY-*` secondary. `kind="signals"` strips never market-hours-CLOSE (prediction/econ run 24/7) ŌĆö wash STALE only on a dead cron (26h), right-pin a green `LIVE` dot. Dual-source render `LABEL K x% P y%` (HO 287 `<SourceTag>` brand-colored K/P), per-slot dim `N/A` when a source is absent (shutdown's Polymarket is a persistent ghost ŌåÆ P N/A). *(Debt ceiling was specced but DROPPED ŌĆö HO 288 found no clean market on either venue; backlog BANKED.)* **HO 274 ŌĆö pinned-left `label`** (MARKETS / ODDS) OUTSIDE the scrolling track (a `label` prop ŌåÆ `.markets-tape-label`, absolute/opaque/right-fade). **HO 274 ŌĆö ┬▒8% implausible-daily-move guard** (`MAX_PLAUSIBLE_DAILY_MOVE_PCT`; FRED `DCOILWTICO` lags multi-day so the cron diffs a fresh value against a week-stale row ŌĆö see oddities).

- `components/MarketsTape.tsx` ŌĆö server, fetches the ticks (catches throw, falls through to the no-data branch).
- `components/MarketsTapeClient.tsx` ŌĆö client, owns the marquee + states. Staleness is computed client-side against real `Date.now()` (server-side staleness would bake into the page-cache TTL and lie at the 26h boundary). **HO 172:** a 60s `setInterval` both re-checks staleness AND polls `GET /api/markets/latest` (the cached `getLatestMarketTicks` JSON), mapping fresh prices onto the existing items keyed by symbol so React reconciles in place. A grouped tape filters the poll payload to its own symbols (via `placeholderSymbols`).
- **Jump-proof geometry (HO 175/176):** the 60s scroll jump was never React identity ŌĆö it was geometry, `translateX(-50%)` against a `width: max-content` track whose width changed whenever a polled value changed an item's rendered width. Fixed by pinning **per-symbol slot widths** (`PRICE_SLOT_CH` in `MarketsTapeClient`, right-aligned + `tabular-nums`) so one set's width is value-invariant; the duration/measure re-runs only on item-count (or stale-branch) change, never on a value update. **HO 179.1:** each marquee half repeats the set `copies = max(2, ceil(container / setWidth))` (measured client-side) so it always fills the viewport ŌĆö and **null-change symbols (first-tick) omit their arrow+change slots** entirely (valued symbols keep the reserved slots ŌåÆ still jump-proof; a symbol's first value is a one-time width settle, not the 60s jump).
- **Motion exception:** the marquee is the one deliberate exception to the dashboard's cursor-blink-only motion rule.
